08:35:57","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 08:35:57","title":"How Landing Pages Impact Quality Score on Every Ad Platform","link":"https://unbounce.com/?p=98247","description":"\n<p>In the world of <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/solutions/use-case/ppc/\">pay-per-click (PPC) advertising</a>, there are few misperceptions as rampant as the ones about <strong>the effects that landing pages have on Quality Score</strong>. That&#8217;s not surprising, given that Quality Score algorithms are &#8220;black boxes&#8221; that play a crucial role in the success of any PPC campaign. We still have very little insight into how Google Ads, Microsoft Advertising (formerly Bing Ads), and the social media advertising platforms calculate and use Quality Score.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Landing pages are often a customer’s first interaction with a brand and set the stage for the relationship going forward. Distilling Quality Score into a number is misleading for PPC advertisers because it undervalues <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/landing-page-articles/why-should-i-use-landing-pages/\">the importance of landing pages</a> on several other crucial components of a campaign, such as brand perception and positioning.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>As a side note, most ad platforms use the term &#8220;Quality Score,&#8221; while others use &#8220;Ad Relevance&#8221; or something similar. For the sake of simplicity, I use Quality Score interchangeably with Ad Relevance and Relevance Score metrics unless otherwise noted. Let&#8217;s get into it!</p>\n\n\n\n<h2><strong>What Is Quality Score &#38; Why Does It Matter to PPC Advertisers?</strong></h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Quality Score is an approximation of your keywords&#8217; and ads&#8217; relevance to your target audience. It&#8217;s usually represented in the ad platforms as a number from 1-10. This dramatically oversimplifies the complex and user-specific Quality Score inputs factored into each ad auction, but it&#8217;s the best we have. Search engines and social media platforms use this metric to <strong>decide which ads to show and how much to charge an advertiser for each click or impression.</strong></p>\n\n\n\n<p>Google Ads pioneered Quality Score in their Ad Rank algorithm to reward advertisers that created relevant ads with a lower cost per click. Advertisers that try to show irrelevant ads to uninterested users may receive a lower Quality Score and have to pay a higher cost per click to remain visible.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>As you can see in the equation below, providing a great user experience to boost your Quality Score can improve your Ad Rank and lower your cost per click. From what we can tell, most PPC platforms use an equation like the one below to determine where your ads appear.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_LPQuailtyScore_formula.jpg\" alt=\"Ad Rank Calculation\" class=\"wp-image-98298\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_LPQuailtyScore_formula.jpg 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_LPQuailtyScore_formula-150x48.jpg 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_LPQuailtyScore_formula-560x179.jpg 560w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_LPQuailtyScore_formula-80x26.jpg 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_LPQuailtyScore_formula-768x245.jpg 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_LPQuailtyScore_formula-650x207.jpg 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_LPQuailtyScore_formula-300x96.jpg 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_LPQuailtyScore_formula-160x51.jpg 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>However, each ad platform treats landing pages differently in their Quality Score equations. Savvy PPC advertisers should understand the nuance of each platform to tailor their campaigns for the best results. As a shorthand, the table below shows the similarities and differences between each major ad platform’s version of Quality Score as well as the associated factors:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_LPQuailtyScore_table.jpg\" alt=\"How Quality Score Is Calculated\" class=\"wp-image-98304\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_LPQuailtyScore_table.jpg 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_LPQuailtyScore_table-150x108.jpg 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_LPQuailtyScore_table-347x250.jpg 347w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_LPQuailtyScore_table-80x58.jpg 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_LPQuailtyScore_table-768x553.jpg 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_LPQuailtyScore_table-650x468.jpg 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_LPQuailtyScore_table-300x216.jpg 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_LPQuailtyScore_table-160x115.jpg 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>In simple terms, here&#8217;s the question platforms are asking when they evaluate your ads against these different attributes:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><strong>Landing Page Experience:</strong> Is your ad&#8217;s landing page relevant to the visitor’s intent and does it help them accomplish their objectives quickly and transparently?</li><li><strong>Ad Click Through Rate/Engagement:</strong> Are your ads clicked as often as competing ads?</li><li><strong>Ad Relevance: </strong>Do your ads align with your audiences’ interests and intent?</li><li><strong>Post-Click Conversion Rate:</strong> Are visitors likely to convert or take meaningful action after clicking your ad?</li><li><strong>Recency:</strong> Are your ads recently published or updated regularly?</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>If the answer to any of these questions is &#8220;no,&#8221; there&#8217;s a good chance your Quality Score is suffering as a result. </p>\n\n\n<div class=\"blog-cta-image-section\" data-ga=\"\"><a href=\"https://unbounce.com/solutions/use-case/ppc/\" target=\"_blank\" data-campaign=\"\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/blog-visual-cta-generic-ppc-yellow.jpg\" alt=\"Landing pages with PPC\" width=\"2260\" height=\"1216\" /></a></div>\n\n\n<h2><strong>How Do Landing Pages Impact Quality Score on Different Platforms?</strong></h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Landing pages are an important part of Quality Score algorithms and, fortunately, are one of the easiest elements of a PPC campaign to control. <strong>The most important part of the “Landing Page Experience” component of Quality Score is providing a positive visitor experience.</strong> Answer their search intent with relevant content, provide <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/page-speed-report/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">lightning-fast page speed</a>, and make sure your site looks great on all screen sizes.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>When done correctly, <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.workshopdigital.com/blog/unbounce-landing-pages-adwords-quality-score/\" target=\"_blank\">landing pages can have a positive impact on Google Ads Quality Score</a>. That means a<strong> lower cost per click and higher conversion rates </strong>when compared to sending traffic to a website. And even though some ad platforms do not explicitly factor landing pages into their Quality Scores, marketers shouldn&#8217;t ignore the improvement in visitor experience and their likelihood of developing a positive association with your brand.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2>1. Google Ads &#8211; Quality Score</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Google Ads’ support content explicitly mentions the <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://support.google.com/google-ads/answer/1659694?hl=en\">importance of landing pages for creating a positive user experience</a>. I want to emphasize the <em>experience</em> portion because most people assume that Google Ads Quality Score only focuses on landing page <em>relevance</em>. Your landing pages must be relevant to keywords and ads that your visitors clicked on, yes, but <strong>it’s </strong><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://support.google.com/google-ads/answer/2404197?hl=en\"><strong>just as important to Google</strong></a><strong> that your landing page loads quickly, is secure, and looks great on all screens.</strong>&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_google_ads.png\" alt=\"Quality Score Attributes - Google Ads\" class=\"wp-image-98314\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_google_ads.png 830w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_google_ads-150x44.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_google_ads-560x166.png 560w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_google_ads-80x24.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_google_ads-768x228.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_google_ads-650x193.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_google_ads-300x89.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_google_ads-160x47.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 830px) 100vw, 830px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<div><p style=\"text-align:center; font-size:80%;\">Here&#8217;s Google Ads explaining how Quality Score is calculated.</p></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Landing pages won’t have any direct impact on the Expected CTR or Ad Relevance components of your Google Ads Quality Score, but the domain and URL you show in your ads may indirectly help or hurt your click-through rates.&#160;</p>\n\n\n<div class=\"curated-tip\">\n    <div class=\"container inner text-left\">\n        <p><strong>Not advertising on Google yet?</strong> Check out our guide to <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/ppc/google-ads-basics/\">getting started with Google Ads</a> and you&#8217;ll have your first PPC campaign up and running in no time. </p>\n    </div>\n</div>\n\n\n<h2>2. Microsoft Advertising &#8211; Quality Score</h2>\n\n\n\n<p><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://help.ads.microsoft.com/apex/index/3/en-us/50894\" target=\"_blank\">Microsoft Advertising Quality Score</a> is nearly identical to Google Ads Quality Score, although they provide significantly less documentation for each of the three components. Unlike Google, Microsoft <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://help.ads.microsoft.com/#apex/3/en/50813/2\" target=\"_blank\">explicitly mentions</a> that the landing page experience factor is “based on how many times customers leave your ad&#8217;s landing page shortly after arriving.” This implies that <strong>lowering your landing page’s bounce rate (among other things) will improve your Quality Score.</strong></p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_ms_advertising.png\" alt=\"Quality Score Attributes - Microsoft Advertising\" class=\"wp-image-98319\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_ms_advertising.png 708w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_ms_advertising-150x26.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_ms_advertising-560x97.png 560w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_ms_advertising-80x14.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_ms_advertising-650x113.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_ms_advertising-300x52.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_ms_advertising-160x28.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 708px) 100vw, 708px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<div><p style=\"text-align:center; font-size:80%;\">Microsoft Advertising&#8217;s writeup on the factors that impact Quality Score.</p></div>\n\n\n\n<p>It is a good idea to monitor your Microsoft Advertising Quality Score, but don’t expect to get much helpful information about individual keywords. In this case, I suggest following the best practices for Google’s Quality Score improvements in the hopes that Microsoft will reward the same efforts.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2>3. Facebook Advertising &#8211; Ad Relevance</h2>\n\n\n\n<p><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.facebook.com/business/help/436113280262012?id=561906377587030\" target=\"_blank\">Facebook’s Ad Relevance</a> is a completely different type of metric than Google’s Quality Score. The three components of Facebook’s Ad Relevance ratings are:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li><strong>Quality Ranking:</strong> A ranking of your ad&#8217;s perceived quality. Quality is measured using feedback on your ads and the post-click experience. Your ad is ranked against ads that competed for the same audience.</li><li><strong>Engagement Rate Ranking:</strong> A ranking of your ad&#8217;s expected engagement rate. Engagement includes all clicks, likes, comments, and shares. Your ad is ranked against ads that competed for the same audience.</li><li><strong>Conversion Rate Ranking:</strong> A ranking of your ad&#8217;s expected <strong>conversion rate</strong>. Your ad is ranked against ads with your optimization goal that competed for the same audience</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>Notably, Facebook’s audience targeting does not rely on search keywords. So it&#8217;s much harder to determine a social user’s intent at any given moment. Many Facebook campaign types also allow users to convert, transact, or engage with content on the platform itself. (So they don’t <em>require</em> a landing page.) In these cases, Facebook relies heavily on the engagement and interactions that happen on its platform to determine if an ad is relevant or not.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>While Facebook Ads&#8217; documentation doesn&#8217;t mention external landing pages, they do reference &#8220;post-click experience&#8221; and &#8220;conversion rate&#8221; in two of the three Ad Relevance factors. Advertisers using Facebook&#8217;s audience and conversion pixels should assume that<strong> Facebook Ads can measure engagement and conversion rates on your websites</strong>. Adjust your landing pages accordingly.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2>4. Twitter Ads &#8211; Ad Score</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Twitter Ads has the least amount of <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://business.twitter.com/en/help/troubleshooting/bidding-and-auctions-faqs.html\" target=\"_blank\">support content related to their Ad Score</a> and no mention of landing pages.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_twitter.png\" alt=\"Quality Score Attributes - Twitter Ads\" class=\"wp-image-98325\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_twitter.png 785w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_twitter-150x27.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_twitter-560x101.png 560w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_twitter-80x14.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_twitter-768x138.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_twitter-650x117.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_twitter-300x54.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/quality_score_twitter-160x29.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 785px) 100vw, 785px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<div><p style=\"text-align:center; font-size:80%;\">The factors that affect your Ad Score on Twitter.</p></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Similar to Facebook Ads, most of Twitter Ads&#8217; conversions happen within their platform in the form of likes, retweets, content engagement, and follows. If Twitter does consider landing page engagement, conversions, or experience as a factor, it doesn&#8217;t seem to influence your campaign performance heavily.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>That said, <strong>pairing your Twitter Ads with dedicated landing pages is still a good idea if you expect to re-engage and convert visitors on your site. </strong>The best Twitter Ads campaigns aren&#8217;t going to reach their full potential if your landing pages don&#8217;t reinforce the positioning (and offers) that you tweet.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2>5. LinkedIn Ads &#8211; Campaign Quality Score</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Oh, LinkedIn. Nothing is easy in LinkedIn Ads, including <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/help/lms/answer/85406/campaign-quality-scores-for-sponsored-content?lang=en\">finding your Campaign Quality Score</a>. Like the other platforms, LinkedIn rates each sponsored content campaign on a 1-10 scale. Unlike the other platforms, they don’t allow you to see your Campaign Quality Score unless you manually export a .csv file of your historical performance.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Once you follow the tedious, eight-step process to export your scores, you’ll find a number in the “Campaign Quality Score” column—but no insights or further detail on how to improve it.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Without this information, the best advice I can give you is to focus on improving your ads’ click-through rates and engagement (likes, shares, etc.). There&#8217;s no mention of landing pages. If you send traffic from your ads to an external site, follow the best practices shared by the other platforms and <strong>put your users’ experience first.</strong> At worst, this will improve your conversion rates. At best, it could boost your Campaign Quality Scores and lower the notoriously high CPCs on LinkedIn Ads.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2><strong>Pay Attention to Quality Score—But Don’t Obsess Over It</strong></h2>\n\n\n\n<p>There are several tried and true methods that will improve your Quality Score with landing pages. Most are focused on enhancing the visitor’s experience and don’t require substantial dev support. Unbounce users can take advantage of <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/product/features/dynamic-text-replacement/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Dynamic Text Replacement</a> to improve relevance and page speed improvements to create lightning-fast experiences.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Your landing pages will (directly and indirectly) influence Quality Score. But the algorithms are opaque, so it&#8217;s impossible to know <em>exactly</em> what&#8217;s working and what isn&#8217;t. We&#8217;ve seen results vary dramatically by industry and campaign type. I recommend thinking about it as a lagging indicator (not a leading metric) of your efforts. Schedule reminders to review your landing page experience scores once per month or once per quarter. Look for progress.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>With a little attention, your landing pages will help take your campaigns to the next level.&#160;</p>\n\n\n<div class=\"blog-cta-image-section\" data-ga=\"\"><a 08:35:57","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 08:35:57","title":"Marketers and Landing Pages: Behind the Scenes for 2020","link":"https://unbounce.com/?p=97489","description":"\n<p>As part of our new <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/conversion-rate-optimization/what-is-a-good-conversion-rate/\" target=\"_blank\">Conversion Benchmark Report</a>, Unbounce ran a survey of marketers, working in dozens of industries, in early 2020. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>We wanted to know about your plans when it comes to running a high-converting campaign—as well as the role played by landing pages in supporting your post-click strategy. How do our expectations line up with the insights revealed by a <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/conversion-rate-optimization/what-is-a-good-conversion-rate/\" target=\"_blank\">machine learning analysis of 19 million conversions</a>? How firm is the average marketer’s grasp on industry conversion rates?&#160;And how satisfied are they with their current performance?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Of course, 2020 didn&#8217;t exactly turn out how anybody expected. (Boy, that&#8217;s an understatement.)&#160;But your answers provide a unique window into the &#8220;best-laid plans&#8221; of marketers and underline how—midway through a <em>beastly</em> year—<strong>some things may have changed in dramatic ways, while others remain tried and true</strong>.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Together with the findings from the report itself, these numbers provide a behind-the-scenes view of what other marketers think when it comes to their landing pages. I thought I&#8217;d share some of the results with you today.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"alignleft size-large\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/blue-rectangle-horizontal.svg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-93558\"/></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2><strong>Takeaway #1: The most popular digital marketing strategy is a diverse one.</strong></h2>\n\n\n\n<p>When asked about budgets, the 400 people we surveyed were evenly split in how much they plan to spend on marketing activities in 2020. Answers ranged from <strong>less than $5,000</strong> to <strong>more than $500,000</strong>, and this didn’t always depend on the size of the business.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>No matter the heft of their wallets, though, marketers also told us they planned to fire on all cylinders by <strong>taking on a wide variety of marketing activities</strong>. Here are the most popular types of campaigns you told us you&#8217;re running this year:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_1.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-97916\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_1.png 874w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_1-150x128.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_1-292x250.png 292w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_1-80x68.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_1-768x657.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_1-650x556.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_1-300x257.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_1-160x137.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 874px) 100vw, 874px\" /><figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">The “Other” category also yields some varied answers, from paper mailers to podcasts to push notifications.</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>In some cases, we expect this mix of activities has changed to match the new normal. A business-as-usual approach to event marketing hasn’t been possible, for instance, and the landscape for PPC and social is <a href=\"https://www.searchenginejournal.com/5-tips-for-managing-ppc-during-the-coronavirus-outbreak/358006/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">different than it was six months ago</a>. (Though PPC experts are nothing if not adaptable.)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>These challenging times don’t mean these activities have been completely abandoned, however. While in-person networking is harder, many companies have found ways to achieve similar goals online by running webinars or digital conferences. (Many say this shift to virtual gatherings will have a <a href=\"https://www.marketingdive.com/news/51-of-marketing-professionals-expect-virtual-events-to-stick-around-surve/579354/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">lasting impact on how they do event marketing</a>.)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Which brings us to another question&#8230;</p>\n\n\n\n<h3>How often are marketers including landing pages as part of their campaigns in 2020?&#160;</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Very often, it turns out. </p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>36.2%</strong> of respondents told us they use them <strong>all of the time,</strong> and <strong>41.8%</strong> said <strong>most of the time</strong>—that’s a whopping <strong>77%</strong> who see landing pages as an essential part of their post-click strategy.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_2.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-97891\" width=\"684\" height=\"585\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_2.png 684w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_2-150x128.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_2-292x250.png 292w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_2-80x68.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_2-650x556.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_2-300x257.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_2-160x137.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 684px) 100vw, 684px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>We surveyed marketers outside our networks, but likely attracted some fans of landing pages (and Unbounce) who may have skewed the results. Still, these responses are an indicator that if you&#8217;re <em>not</em> using landing pages to support your campaigns, you&#8217;re in the minority.</p>\n\n\n<div class=\"curated-tip\">\n    <div class=\"container inner text-left\">\n        <p><strong>New to landing pages?</strong> One reason they appeal to so many marketers is that they help you squeeze more conversions out of your existing ad budget. If we’ve piqued your interest, take a look at our guide to <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/how-to-create-a-landing-page/\" target=_blank>creating your first Unbounce landing page</a> to learn more about how you can get started. </p>\n    </div>\n</div>\n\n\n<h2><strong>Takeaway #2: Marketers are doing a whole lot with their landing pages.&#160;</strong></h2>\n\n\n\n<p>So, yes, marketers are using landing pages quite often.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>When it comes to <em>how</em> they’re using them, we naturally expected lead-gen activities to top the charts. That&#8217;s still true, but it was also surprising how many respondents said they also use landing pages to connect more directly with prospects by scheduling appointments (<strong>42%</strong>) and phone calls (<strong>37.2%</strong>).&#160;Here&#8217;s how it breaks down:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_3.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-97894\" width=\"940\" height=\"979\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_3.png 940w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_3-144x150.png 144w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_3-240x250.png 240w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_3-77x80.png 77w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_3-768x800.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_3-650x677.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_3-300x312.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_3-154x160.png 154w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 940px) 100vw, 940px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Four years ago, when we were working on the first version of the <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/conversion-benchmark-report/\">Conversion Benchmark Report</a>, we focused our analysis entirely on lead gen because the overwhelming majority of landing pages on our platform served that purpose.<strong> That’s no longer the case. </strong></p>\n\n\n\n<p>This year’s findings reveal that what marketers consider to be a conversion has diversified. A conversion can look <em>very different</em> depending on your business, your customers, and your goals. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>For example, while CTAs related to ecommerce (like showing off merchandise or adding a product to cart) are still less common than, say, calls to download an ebook, the popularity of these use cases continues to grow. As competition increases and <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/campaign-strategy/how-to-start-online-business-quickly/\">more brick-and-mortar businesses move online</a>, we expect more marketers to adopt <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/conversion-rate-optimization/pre-cart-landing-pages/\">pre-cart landing pages</a>. These let them tell better stories about their products or frame their offers in more compelling ways.</p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\"/>\n\n\n\n<h2><strong>Takeaway #3: When it comes to reaching their conversion potential, marketers are an ambitious bunch.&#160;</strong></h2>\n\n\n\n<p>In advance of publishing the benchmark data, we were curious about what marketers think is an <em>average </em>conversion rate in their industry and what kinds of conversion rates they&#8217;d be satisfied with achieving.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>As expected, you’ve got high—but, crucially, <em>not</em> unrealistic—expectations about how you want your landing pages to perform. First, here’s how respondents told us they think the average page performs in their industry:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_4-1.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-97917\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_4-1.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_4-1-150x97.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_4-1-388x250.png 388w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_4-1-80x52.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_4-1-768x495.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_4-1-650x419.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_4-1-300x194.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_4-1-160x103.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Marketers rarely <em>expect</em> conversion rates over 10%. More than two-thirds of them told us that the averages in their industry are likely below that impenetrable ceiling. (As we&#8217;ll see, their instincts aren&#8217;t wrong.)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>But here’s where you told us you&#8217;d <em>like</em> to be:&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_5.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-97918\" width=\"1000\" height=\"645\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_5.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_5-150x97.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_5-388x250.png 388w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_5-80x52.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_5-768x495.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_5-650x419.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_5-300x194.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_5-160x103.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Clearly, marketers crave big numbers when it comes to conversion rates. If we total the numbers, <strong>71.8% </strong>of marketers told us they’re trying to achieve conversion rates of <strong>11%</strong> or higher. Many have their sights set even higher than that! </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Lofty goals like these are good—<em>great</em> even. And our results show they’re definitely achievable, but probably not without knowing your audience very well and taking the time to test and continuously optimize your landing pages and campaigns. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>So&#8230;</p>\n\n\n\n<h3>How do landing pages in your industry <em>actually </em>perform?</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Drumroll, please&#8230; <img src=\"https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/12.0.0-1/72x72/1f941.png\" alt=\"🥁\" class=\"wp-smiley\" style=\"height: 1em; max-height: 1em;\" /></p>\n\n\n\n<p>According to our analysis of 34 thousand landing pages, the <strong>average landing page</strong> <strong>converts at 9.7% (or 3.2%, expressed as a median</strong>).</p>\n\n\n\n<p>That&#8217;s not the whole story, though. Some industries perform much better than others. For example, the finance and insurance industries convert at <strong>11.6% (average)</strong>, while real estate achieves<strong> average conversion rates of</strong> <strong>6.2%</strong>. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>And when we decided to isolate the top quartile in our conversion data—that&#8217;s fancy talk for focusing on the <em>top 25%</em> of performers—we also see much more drool-worthy conversion rates. In finance and insurance, chart-topping pages convert closer to 26%! (So people who told us they wouldn&#8217;t be satisfied with anything less aren&#8217;t dreaming. There are campaigns and marketers achieving those kinds of results right now.)</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/home-improvement-desktop-graph-1.jpg\" alt=\"Conversion Rate by Home Improvement Type Graph\" class=\"wp-image-94772\" width=\"1082\" height=\"670\"/><figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">This graph from the Conversion Benchmark Report shows the median (rather than average) conversion rates for four subcategories in the home improvement industry. </figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>These are just a few generalities. In <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/conversion-benchmark-report/\" target=\"_blank\">the report,</a> you&#8217;ll find the specific benchmarks related to 16 industries, including SaaS, e-comm, agencies, and business services. You can also read insights about how long your pages should be, what reading level you should target, what calls-to-action are most popular, and which emotions relate to more conversions.</p>\n\n\n<div class=\"curated-tip\">\n    <div class=\"container inner text-left\">\n        <p><strong>Why&#8217;d we create the report?</strong> More than just benchmarks, the data-derived insights from the <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/conversion-benchmark-report/\" target=_blank>Conversion Benchmark Report</a> will help you pair your savvy with AI to create the highest-converting campaigns of your career.  It&#8217;s part of the <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/conversion-intelligence/\" target=_blank><strong>Unbounce Conversion Intelligence<img src=\"https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/12.0.0-1/72x72/2122.png\" alt=\"™\" class=\"wp-smiley\" style=\"height: 1em; max-height: 1em;\" /></strong></a> mission to bring marketers new ways to optimize and level up their skills.</p>\n    </div>\n</div>\n\n\n<h2><strong>Takeaway #4: Delivering the right landing page for the right audience remains a challenge.</strong></h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Let&#8217;s sum up what we&#8217;ve learned so far. Marketers have big ambitions for their landing pages, and they’re looking to do even more with them in 2020. We also saw that the <em>best-performing</em> landing pages routinely hit double-digit conversion rates. (Yowza.)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>So, what’s holding the rest of &#8217;em back? We wanted to know where our respondents saw room to improve their landing pages, and here’s what they told us:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_6.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-97920\" width=\"865\" height=\"758\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_6.png 865w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_6-150x131.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_6-285x250.png 285w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_6-80x70.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_6-768x673.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_6-650x570.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_6-300x263.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Graph_6-160x140.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 865px) 100vw, 865px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>It wasn’t deliberate, but it seems to me that the answers here fall into four broad categories:&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>First, there are <strong>issues with optimization</strong>. Marketers feel they don&#8217;t have time to optimize their pages using <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/landing-page-articles/what-is-ab-testing/\" target=\"_blank\">A/B testing</a>. Sometimes they may not have the data or expertise to make meaningful choices when it comes to improving their conversion rates.</li><li>Second, <strong>matching the right page to the right audience </strong>can be tricky. Fixing it can involve traffic optimizations further up the funnel. But how do you <em>also </em>make sure that each visitor hits the landing page that&#8217;s right for them? </li><li>Third, whether it&#8217;s a matter of talent or time, sometimes marketers don&#8217;t feel like <strong>the copy and design</strong> on their pages are effective. (Testing could help, yes. But see #1 on this list.) For small businesses, marketers may have to play too many roles. And they may not have access to learning material that helps them improve.</li><li>And fourth are <strong>technical hurdles</strong>, like slow loading times or ensuring pages look perfect on different devices. (These made up the &#8220;Other&#8221; category above.) In this case, marketers have risen to the challenge of building lighter, more mobile-friendly experiences.</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>Today&#8217;s marketers have a lot on their plate—you could say they&#8217;re young, scrappy, and hungry—but that doesn&#8217;t mean they&#8217;re not looking for easy ways to step up their game.</p>\n\n\n\n<p style=\"background-color:#ededed\" class=\"has-background\"><strong>How&#8217;d we get these numbers?</strong> We fielded the Unbounce Conversion Benchmark Survey between December 2019 and February 2020. To ensure a healthy sample size, we surveyed 439 people. After a few qualifying questions, we paired it down 400 respondents who identified as marketers.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2>How can marketers overcome these challenges?</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>When it comes to getting the most conversions from your landing pages, we&#8217;ve been talking a lot about a shift in mindset we&#8217;re calling <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/news/introducing-conversion-intelligence/\" target=\"_blank\">Conversion Intelligence</a>. Again and again, we&#8217;ve seen evidence that better performance isn&#8217;t an accident. It&#8217;s the result of <strong>continuously fine-tunin<b>g</b></strong><b> each element of your campaigns</b>. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>But when marketers often do this optimization work on their own, they quickly run up against limits—of time and money, of expertise, of insight. By <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/marketing-ai/artificial-intelligence-will-change-how-you-do-marketing-in-2021/\">pairing your expertise with Artificial Intelligence</a>, you can overcome these limits. You can create and optimize the highest-converting campaigns possible.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/conversion-intelligence-brain.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-96535\" width=\"1000\" height=\"593\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/conversion-intelligence-brain.png 1999w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/conversion-intelligence-brain-150x89.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/conversion-intelligence-brain-421x250.png 421w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/conversion-intelligence-brain-80x47.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/conversion-intelligence-brain-768x456.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/conversion-intelligence-brain-1536x911.png 1536w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/conversion-intelligence-brain-1000x593.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/conversion-intelligence-brain-650x386.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/conversion-intelligence-brain-300x178.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/conversion-intelligence-brain-160x95.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Our teams are working to share opportunities you couldn’t spot without the processing power of a machine. For now, you can check out the <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/conversion-benchmark-report/\" target=\"_blank\">Conversion Benchmark Report</a>. Starting with the benchmarks,  dig into your industry. Use the machine-derived insights about reading ease, word count, and sentiment to create higher-converting pages. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Better yet, <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/marketing-ai/optimize-with-smart-traffic-landing-page-variants/\">build a low-commitment (as in, quick and easy) variant or two</a> based on the insights in the CBR, then flip on <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/product/smart-traffic/\">Smart Traffic</a> and see how they perform. This feature uses machine learning to <strong>automatically match each and every visitor to the landing page most likely to convert.</strong> There&#8217;s no need to babysit it or declare a champion variant, and it never stops learning.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Using Smart Traffic is a quick win, especially if you don&#8217;t have the time or traffic for the traditional A/B testing. It needs just a little bit of attention to get it up and running on your most important pages. <strong>All you need to do is build a few variants, and turn it on.</strong> We see an average lift in conversions of 20% for customers who use it, so it&#8217;s very much worth the small effort.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"alignleft size-large\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/pink-rectangle-horizontal.svg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-93559\"/></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2><strong>Finding a New Normal</strong></h2>\n\n\n\n<p>The Conversion Benchmark Report Survey was a bit of informal market research before starting on an intimidating project. But your responses also helped us enrich the quantitative data (generated with the help of AI) with some good old-fashioned human intuition. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>It continues to be a challenging year, and we’ll run a follow-up survey to see how things have changed for you in 2021. But, for now, I’m curious: how have your plans changed? Have you adjusted? Have you pivoted? <em>Swerved</em>?&#160;Tempered your expectations? Adapted your existing campaigns to the new normal? Found new opportunities even?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Let me know in the comments.</p>\n\n\n<div class=\"blog-cta-image-section\" data-ga=\"\"><a href=\"https://unbounce.com/conversion-benchmark-report/\" 08:35:57","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 08:35:57","title":"8 High-Converting Lead Generation Landing Page Examples to Inspire Yours","link":"https://unbounce.com/?p=96980","description":"\n<p>Ask and you shall receive, right?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Not so much when it comes to your visitors’ email addresses. You likely don’t have to look further than your own inbox to see why—there’s no shortage of companies ready to flood you with their latest and greatest offers. Which means people are wiser to marketing tactics and, understandably, more discerning than ever about who they give their contact information out to. They need more than a blank form field. They need to clearly see the value on the other side of that “sign me up” button.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>That value is communicated through more than just copy. (Though messaging is indeed very important! Signed, a totally unbiased copywriter.) <strong>The how, where, and why of what you’re asking is what creates a compelling overall experience for the visitor.</strong> One that shows you understand and respect their needs. And that you’re offering something really great to make trading their email a total no-brainer.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>It’s about showing <em>and </em>telling.</strong> And in the spirit of show and tell, we’re going to do just that. Below, you’ll find eight lead generation landing page examples from Unbounce customers that prove effective lead gen comes in all <em>forms.</em>&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/milhouseshowandtell.gif\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-96981\"/></figure></div>\n\n\n<div class=\"editors-note\">\n    <p>Just getting started collecting subscribers? Read our step-by-step <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/campaign-strategy/how-to-build-an-email-list/\" rel=\"noopener\">guide to building an email list</a> from scratch. </p>\n</div>\n\n\n<h2><strong>Steal Some Lead Gen Landing Page Tips From These Clever Unbounce Customers </strong></h2>\n\n\n\n<h3>Vancouver Island University</h3>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><a class=\"fancybox iframelpexamples\" href=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/VIU-Full-2020.png\" target=\"_blank\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/VIU-Crop.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-97150\" width=\"1000\" height=\"411\"></a><figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">Click to see VIU’s “Worth It” landing page in its entirety.</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.viu.ca/?v&#38;utm_expid=.QBuox4PKQQCyLP4Lb15WfA.1&#38;utm_referrer=\" target=\"_blank\">Vancouver Island University</a> knows one of the biggest concerns for many students (besides dodging those 8:00 a.m. class slots) is paying tuition. And that said investment in education brings other concerns along with it, like which field or studies should they put that investment <em>toward</em>, and what’s their career potential once it&#8217;s been made?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Instead of leaving prospective pupils to figure it out on their own, VIU created the “Worth It” campaign centered around this lead generation landing page. Not only does it give students information to help answer those questions, it offers up a chance to win $2,500 credited toward their Fall 2020 tuition. <strong>And their nine percent conversion rate of nearly 35,000 visitors, which is well above the <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/conversion-benchmark-report/#education\">education industry median</a>, proves their lead gen efforts are paying off.&#160;</strong></p>\n\n\n\n<p>Making sure not to bury the lede, VIU focused on the clearest incentive—that sweet, stone cold cash—and put its entry form right at the top of the page. Surrounded by colorful graphics and laid over a photo of fresh-faced students gathered on a beach, a cheerful, people-centric message is instantly communicated, featuring the coastal Vancouver Island backdrop that sets VIU’s campus apart from others. <strong>So there’s already a huge value proposition served up in the hero section, before visitors even start scrolling to the rest of the goodies below.</strong></p>\n\n\n\n<p>Those goodies being a wealth of resources, delivered through engaging video, statistics, easily digestible summaries, and a straightforward Q&#38;A format that voices common concerns students have followed by all of the programs, benefits, and opportunities VIU offers to help and guide them. As they continue down the landing page, more general and experiential benefits of a VIU education are showcased—like small class sizes, an inclusive community, and laid back “island life” on one of the world’s most beautiful natural playgrounds.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The VIU team (of only six!) who worked on this campaign drove traffic through a number of channels, from paid advertising on Facebook and YouTube to social media sharing to traditional print ads at ferry terminals and their local airport. Not surprisingly, given the nature of their target audience, most of their traffic came from mobile devices.</p>\n\n\n\n<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote\"><p><em>“What helped us with conversion rates was that Unbounce is such a mobile-friendly platform. The bulk of the traffic generated for this campaign was from mobile. We had a lot of flexibility on how things were displayed on different screen sizes and this enabled us to better optimize the page and convert more leads.”</em></p><cite>Christine Johnson, Digital Marketing Specialist, Vancouver Island University&#160;</cite></blockquote>\n\n\n\n<p>The bottom line—they crushed their bottom line. With a combination of audience insight, solution-oriented empathy, informational value, smart targeting, and an undeniably compelling call to action, they <strong>exceeded their original goal of 500 leads to bring in over 3,100. </strong>Which gives a whole new meaning to the “Worth It” campaign.</p>\n\n\n\n<h3><strong>ckbk</strong></h3>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/CKBKcopy.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-97470\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/CKBKcopy.png 1440w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/CKBKcopy-54x150.png 54w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/CKBKcopy-90x250.png 90w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/CKBKcopy-29x80.png 29w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/CKBKcopy-768x2131.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/CKBKcopy-554x1536.png 554w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/CKBKcopy-738x2048.png 738w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/CKBKcopy-1000x2774.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/CKBKcopy-650x1803.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/CKBKcopy-300x832.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/CKBKcopy-58x160.png 58w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1440px) 100vw, 1440px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.ckbk.com/\" target=\"_blank\">ckbk</a> is a digital cookbook service that brings the world’s best recipes online, making classic and contemporary cookbook content available to members in one convenient place. As a subscription-based business, landing pages are key to ckbk’s marketing in order to grow their email lists and drive more signups.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Here, they’ve done something a little different than your typical lead generation strategy by incentivizing registrations with an extended free trial voucher. This landing page not only acts as a gateway for visitors to enter the code they’ve been given, referred, or seen promoted online, it also serves as additional advertising for all of the content and services they offer.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Which is exactly what makes this page so compelling—<strong>a showcase of benefits through messaging, video, testimonial, and imagery</strong>. Just below a warm and inviting hero image (anybody else craving some fresh-baked bread right now?) showing a real-life recipe displayed on a mobile device is a summary of membership value alongside a short promotional video. As you scroll down, the features and benefits—like diversity of recipes, filters for skill level and dietary requirements, the ability to create your own “collections,” and more—are plainly laid out to show visitors all the goods they’re in for and address any concerns or questions you may have before signing up. Complete with a bright, eye-catching (and mouthwatering) image gallery of just some of the cookbooks included.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>They also clearly know just how important building trust is, especially depending on the level of information you may be asking visitors to share. Endorsements from award-winning chefs and travel writers, press from recognizable publications, and a note that a membership can be cancelled anytime—including during the extended free trial—all help to reassure visitors they’re in good hands.</p>\n\n\n\n<p><em>PS. The fine people of ckbk have offered a voucher for any Unbounce blog foodies interested in trying out their service! Use “COOKBOOKSFOR30DAYS”</em> <em>to claim your extended trial </em><a href=\"https://join.ckbk.com/redeem/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><em>here</em></a><em>.</em></p>\n\n\n\n<h3><strong>Condair</strong></h3>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Condair.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-96985\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Condair.png 1440w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Condair-103x150.png 103w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Condair-171x250.png 171w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Condair-55x80.png 55w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Condair-768x1123.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Condair-1051x1536.png 1051w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Condair-1401x2048.png 1401w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Condair-1000x1462.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Condair-650x950.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Condair-300x439.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Condair-109x160.png 109w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1440px) 100vw, 1440px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Commercial and industrial humidification and evaporative cooling products may not sound <em>too</em> sexy to the average bear—but the average bear isn’t <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.condairgroup.com/\" target=\"_blank\">Condair’s</a> target audience. <strong>And with a conversion rate of 83%</strong> on this lead generation landing page for a free desktop hygrometer, they clearly know just what that target audience wants (to the tune of over 2,800 conversions).</p>\n\n\n\n<p>This targeting is what makes Condair’s offer so clever as a lead generation strategy. Everyone loves to get a little something for free, but they’re not giving just <em>anything </em>away. Instead of a more typical “swag” item like a coffee mug or t-shirt—which, while still great, are more generic items any business can customize—they’re dishing out freebies that are perfectly aligned with the products and services they offer, and the wants and needs of their prospects.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Visitors to this page are likely already problem aware, somewhat solution aware, and probably in some stage of evaluation. <strong>It’s super smart for Condair to offer a gift in exchange for their information so they can get in direct contact, and to use page real estate for additional form fields that help qualify leads</strong> instead of trying to dazzle them with superfluous design or slick photography that doesn’t hold much weight for their prospects. Instead, they’ve kept their offer and landing page itself simple, making space to ask the kind of questions they need to in order to best serve that individual. That said, they don’t go overboard with form fields—there are just enough questions to get a context for that visitor’s needs while keeping their time, and value of their exchange, in mind.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The benefit is three-fold: Condair gets a contact portal and wealth of data for prospects who may have otherwise anonymously left their site, a relationship is instantly established through reciprocity, and said prospects get a cool little present <em>before they even become</em> Condair customers.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<h3><strong>National Sewing Circle</strong></h3>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/NSS.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-96986\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/NSS.png 1440w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/NSS-150x93.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/NSS-404x250.png 404w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/NSS-80x49.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/NSS-768x475.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/NSS-1000x618.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/NSS-650x402.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/NSS-300x185.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/NSS-160x99.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1440px) 100vw, 1440px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>The folks at <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.nationalsewingcircle.com/\" target=\"_blank\">National Sewing Circle</a> (and their marketing agency, <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.tnmarketing.com/\" target=\"_blank\">TN Marketing</a>) are seasoned pros at effective lead generation. We’ve featured their work before in a post on great <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/conversion-rate-optimization/14-inspiring-popup-design-examples-to-help-grow-your-online-business/\">popup examples</a>, and couldn’t pass up another opportunity to do so when we discovered how well this lead gen landing page was performing.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Don’t let that seemingly innocuous little carrot fool you—this page packs a serious <strong>conversion punch at 88% of over 3,400 visitors</strong>. Catering to a thriving and active community of sewing enthusiasts, they’ve chosen to offer a cute, fun, and broadly-applicable pattern with an incredibly low barrier to entry. Much like Condair in the previous example, National Sewing Circle understands the balance of give and take, asking only for an email address to “unlock your download.” From there, they can <strong>nurture those leads through <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/solutions/use-case/email-marketing/\">email marketing</a> and show how much value they can deliver</strong> beyond this humble yet hardworking carrot.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/carrotworkout.gif\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-96987\"/></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>And get this—it’s one of <em>many.</em> The simplicity of this landing page makes it extra easy to duplicate with minimal customizations, as well as giving it a clean, clutter-free appearance. And since National Sewing Circle knows there’s (usually) no such thing as too many leads, they’ve made it part of a themed package of individual patterns. The landing page below, also created in Unbounce, links out to each pattern’s respective download page, all with similarly high conversion rates.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p><a href=\"https://ueni.com/en-us/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">UENI</a>, which provides marketing and advertising services to small businesses, proves <strong>anticipation can be a powerful thing</strong> with this relatively vague, yet high-converting landing page targeted at ecommerce clients.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>One of the primary use cases for lead generation landing pages is drumming up excitement <em>before</em> a business, product, service, announcement, or whatever the case may be, has even come to fruition. It’s a way to<strong> get the word out early while building a list of subscribers, allowing you to gauge interest before going to market and create a more solid launchpad for when you do.</strong> We’ve used this strategy before for Unbounce campaigns, and I have to admit that launch day is a<em> lot </em>less nerve wracking when you already have a list of people who’ve essentially told you they’re excited to see what you’ve got.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>In this case, UENI’s applied a light hand in copy and design to beautifully capture a feeling of “mystery” while giving enough detail away to intrigue the right clients. Though the page may seem sparse, its polished design, saturated, high-contrast colors, and use of negative background space <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/landing-page-examples/how-ecommerce-company-packlane-delivers-on-brand-targeted-campaigns-with-custom-landing-pages/\">reflect their brand</a> and a certain level of quality one can expect from them (even in its simplest form).</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The copy is doing a lot of heavy lifting, too. In a handful of sentences, they’ve managed to communicate everything they need to about who this offer is for, why it’s great—as the headline claims—and what makes it special (exclusive access). It’s a strong case for swapping out nothing more than your email address. And at a <strong>56% conversion rate,</strong> it seems a lot of people are <em>already</em> sold.</p>\n\n\n<div class=\"editors-note\">\n    <p>Learn the ins and outs of high-converting <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/conversion-rate-optimization/ecommerce-landing-page-examples-sales/\" rel=\"noopener\">ecommerce landing pages</a> from 27 real-word examples.</p>\n</div>\n\n\n<h3><strong>Frank &#38; Dick</strong></h3>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/VB.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-96993\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/VB.png 1440w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/VB-119x150.png 119w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/VB-199x250.png 199w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/VB-64x80.png 64w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/VB-768x966.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/VB-1221x1536.png 1221w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/VB-1000x1258.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/VB-650x817.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/VB-300x377.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/VB-127x160.png 127w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1440px) 100vw, 1440px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.frankanddick.no/\" target=\"_blank\">Frank &#38; Dick</a> is a digital advertising and media agency based in Oslo, Norway, that specializes in ecommerce for mid-to-large businesses.
