22_e094db9e1b450484.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598315757678},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 08:35:57","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 08:35:57","title":"Creating Signup Pages That Convert (With 12 Examples)","link":"https://unbounce.com/?p=96991","description":"\n<p>&#8220;<strong>Attention!</strong>&#8220;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>You’ve heard the word before. Marketers, copywriters, and salespeople talk about <em>attention</em> all the time. It’s like a nervous tic, always sitting on the tip of the tongue.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>It&#8217;s curious, though, because another word that marketers <em>don&#8217;t often </em>use is &#8220;patience.&#8221; And <strong>patience is just as important</strong>. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Sure, our first objective is to gain the <em>attention</em> of our prospects. But with signup pages, it&#8217;s also about making that registration process as painless and as easy as possible.&#160;In other words, it&#8217;s not enough just to get your visitors&#8217; attention⁠—you shouldn&#8217;t test their patience either. Not with additional questions. Not with confusing copy. Not with incongruent design. As UX expert Steve Krug once famously put it, &#8220;Don&#8217;t make me think.&#8221;&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Today we&#8217;re going to cover <strong>12 examples of signup pages that get both patience and attention right</strong>, with commentary by yours truly. But before we get our hands dirty, let&#8217;s take a closer look at what a signup page is.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"alignleft size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/blue-rectangle-horizontal.svg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-93558\" width=\"25\" height=\"5\"/></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2><strong>What&#8217;s a Signup Page?</strong></h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Simply put, a signup page is a type of landing page with a primary conversion goal to drive registrations.&#160;These can occur on the landing page itself, or the page can prime visitors before prompting them to enter an account creation flow.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Now, you may be saying to yourself, &#8220;But I’m already driving traffic to my website. Do I <em>really</em> need a separate signup page?&#8221;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Let&#8217;s make a comparison. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>When someone lands on your website&#8217;s homepage, they could have come from one of many channels (like an organic search or by clicking a backlink in someone else&#8217;s content.) They&#8217;re checking you out, yes, but they may not be there to buy. They might not even know what you&#8217;re offering or what you do. Your visitors are curious, maybe. Intrigued? Possibly. But will they fill out a contact form? Don&#8217;t count on it. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>When you run ads, though, your main goal is often to get your visitors to convert. For this reason, it makes much more sense to send them to a landing page that is <strong>specifically designed to get them to sign up</strong> instead of a generic homepage full of links and other distractions. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/austin-distel-goFBjlQiZFU-unsplash.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-97344\" width=\"960\" height=\"640\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/austin-distel-goFBjlQiZFU-unsplash.jpg 1920w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/austin-distel-goFBjlQiZFU-unsplash-150x100.jpg 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/austin-distel-goFBjlQiZFU-unsplash-375x250.jpg 375w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/austin-distel-goFBjlQiZFU-unsplash-80x53.jpg 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/austin-distel-goFBjlQiZFU-unsplash-768x512.jpg 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/austin-distel-goFBjlQiZFU-unsplash-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/austin-distel-goFBjlQiZFU-unsplash-1000x667.jpg 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/austin-distel-goFBjlQiZFU-unsplash-650x433.jpg 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/austin-distel-goFBjlQiZFU-unsplash-300x200.jpg 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/austin-distel-goFBjlQiZFU-unsplash-160x107.jpg 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 960px) 100vw, 960px\" /><figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">Photo by <a href=\"https://unsplash.com/@austindistel?utm_source=unsplash&#38;utm_medium=referral&#38;utm_content=creditCopyText\">Austin Distel</a> on <a href=\"https://unsplash.com/?utm_source=unsplash&#38;utm_medium=referral&#38;utm_content=creditCopyText\">Unsplash</a></figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2>When should I use a signup page?</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>If you&#8217;re running paid ads, you should be using a signup page. That goes for PPC ads and social media ads like Facebook, LinkedIn, and Twitter, or if you&#8217;re running email campaigns. In all cases, <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/solutions/use-case/email-marketing/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">using dedicated landing pages</a> to drive traffic is an easy way to boost conversions.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>With SaaS, especially, remember the importance of patience. It&#8217;s crucial here because testing your target audience&#8217;s patience will cost you—a lot. No one bounces faster than a first-time SaaS user. That&#8217;s why you must ease them in. <strong>Sequenced pages can help you achieve this goal by making the experience seamless, focused, and pleasant.</strong></p>\n\n\n\n<p>Two other elements are vital to keep in mind. First, grant your users small victories, in the beginning, to give them a sense of empowerment. And, second, be sure to show them tons of value early on. Have them perceive the value of your tool, specifically <em>for them</em>. How do you create these little <em>Aha! </em>moments? By having them apply what they learned easily, and by getting them to experience the results for themselves.</p>\n\n\n<div class=\"curated-tip\">\n    <div class=\"container inner text-left\">\n        <p><strong>Wanna learn how other SaaS marketers use landing pages to connect with customers?</strong> See how you can get a handle on your business and achieve unprecedented growth in <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/saas-optimization-guide/\" target=_blank>our guide for SaaS marketers from Talia Wolf</a>.</p>\n    </div>\n</div>\n\n\n<h2>Create a signup page that&#8217;ll knock their socks off.</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Like most landing pages, a high-converting signup page must have some <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/landing-page-articles/the-anatomy-of-a-landing-page/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">essential elements</a>, like:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>A clear benefit-driven headline</li><li>A subheading that drives home the point</li><li>A fantastic (and relevant) hero image </li><li>A compelling call-to-action &#160;</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>&#8220;But wait.&#8221; Yes, you there with your hand raised. &#8220;Where’s the  form?&#8221;&#160;<em>Exactly</em>! </p>\n\n\n\n<p>A great signup page is one that might as well be yelling, &#8220;Look, ma. No hands!&#8221; You want to keep the <em>f-f-f-friction </em>to a minimum, either by keeping your form as short as possible or even hiding it until the right might moment. (Some smart examples of this tactic below.)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>You do this by having them click on the call-to-action, no fields. And <em>voilà</em>! A form appears, seemingly out of thin air. From there, you&#8217;ve got options. Will you lead them down a multi-page sequence? Or will you collect the email and get them to log onto your platform, where they’ll be prompted to follow dopamine-triggering queues? Or will you email them and start nurturing them that way?&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The best way to learn is to see these principles in action, though. Let’s dig deeper into how to create a signup page by going over some Unbounce-certified examples below.</p>\n\n\n<div class=\"blog-cta-image-section\" data-ga=\"\"><a href=\"https://unbounce.com/solutions/industry/saas/\" target=\"_blank\" data-campaign=\"[General] Unbounce for SaaS\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/large-SaaS-Blog-Visual-CTA_2.png\" alt=\"Find out how to build high-converting Unbounce pages without disrupting a single developer\" width=\"1000\" height=\"538\" /></a></div>\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"alignleft size-large is-resized\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/pink-rectangle-horizontal.svg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-93559\" width=\"25\" height=\"6\"/></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2><strong>12 Great Signup Pages Created by Unbounce Customers</strong></h2>\n\n\n\n<p>As the name suggests, an excellent registration page follows all the principles of a great landing page but uses them to get people to fill out your form. Since we have a dozen examples to review, let&#8217;s focus on actionable takeaways.</p>\n\n\n\n<h3>1. Ruby shows incredible focus.</h3>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><a class=\"fancybox iframelpexamples\" href=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/ruby-full-signup-page.png\" target=\"_blank\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example.png\" alt=\"Screenshot Ruby signup pages\" class=\"wp-image-97349\" width=\"1182\" height=\"597\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example.png 2363w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-150x76.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-495x250.png 495w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-80x40.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-768x388.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-1536x776.png 1536w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-2048x1035.png 2048w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-1000x505.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-650x328.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-300x152.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-160x81.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1182px) 100vw, 1182px\" /></a><figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">Image courtesy of <a href=\"https://www.ruby.com\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Ruby</a>. (Click to see the whole thing.)</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.ruby.com\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Ruby</a> is a virtual receptionist and chat company that gets the power of branding. Their gorgeous above-the-fold setup for this landing page is a perfect example of signup done right. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>First of all, the headline is direct. Make more sales when people reach out to you. They promise to help you create &#8220;happy customers&#8221; while you’re at it.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The body copy is equally clear. The first sentence (&#8220;Missed calls are costing you customers&#8221;) is a swift punch to the gut. Hit ‘em where the pain point is. Then, tie that to your offer, with a bow. Well done.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>And look at that image. The yellow sticks out like a broken thumb, and the caller’s gripping the phone. There&#8217;s a clear gap between the caller and the target audience, symbolizing silence. Her expression. What is she <em>thinking</em>? <strong>This isn&#8217;t your typical stock image.</strong></p>\n\n\n\n<p>The two buttons? I&#8217;d probably <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/landing-page-articles/what-is-ab-testing/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">A/B test</a> this setup against a single button, since you can easily find their phone number on the top right-hand corner. It might yield higher conversion rates.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Also, comparing this signup page with <a href=\"https://www.ruby.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Ruby&#8217;s homepage</a> illustrates the different approach you need to take with your landing pages:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Homepage-Above-the-Fold-Comparison.png\" alt=\"Screenshot of Ruby homepage\" class=\"wp-image-97350\" width=\"1260\" height=\"629\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Homepage-Above-the-Fold-Comparison.png 2520w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Homepage-Above-the-Fold-Comparison-150x75.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Homepage-Above-the-Fold-Comparison-501x250.png 501w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Homepage-Above-the-Fold-Comparison-80x40.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Homepage-Above-the-Fold-Comparison-768x383.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Homepage-Above-the-Fold-Comparison-1536x767.png 1536w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Homepage-Above-the-Fold-Comparison-2048x1022.png 2048w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Homepage-Above-the-Fold-Comparison-1000x499.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Homepage-Above-the-Fold-Comparison-650x324.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Homepage-Above-the-Fold-Comparison-300x150.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Ruby-Homepage-Above-the-Fold-Comparison-160x80.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1260px) 100vw, 1260px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Fair headline, right? Unlike the signup page, though, it ain&#8217;t about the target audience at all. &#8220;Meet Ruby&#8221; sounds a lot like something you’d say when introducing someone at a party. The body copy focuses on the company too. And the CTA? &#8220;Watch <em>OUR </em>Video.&#8221;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>But the most significant difference lies in all those menu options. Buttons are popping out at you from almost every corner. That&#8217;s five buttons I get exposed to even before I start scrolling. <em>Everything </em>is calling for my attention, and I&#8217;m more likely to begin exploring than to convert.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>This works for a homepage, of course. It&#8217;s beckoning us to browse and get to know Ruby. But Ruby&#8217;s signup page had a<strong> much tighter focus in its messaging suited to converting traffic from a paid campaign</strong>.</p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\"/>\n\n\n\n<h3>2. GraphicsZoo stays true with a gorgeous landing page.</h3>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><a class=\"fancybox iframelpexamples\" href=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/graphicszoo-full-signup.png\" target=\"_blank\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/graphicszoo-signup-page-above-the-fold-example.gif\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-97352\"/></a><figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">Image courtesy of <a href=\"https://www.graphicszoo.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">GraphicsZoo</a>. (Click to see the whole thing.)</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.graphicszoo.com/\" target=\"_blank\">GraphicsZoo</a> offers white-label design services for agencies.&#160;Its signup page is sizzling hot in its simplicity. As a white-label graphic design service, they <em>get</em> landing page design.&#160;The GIF above gives you a sneak peek of the platform. That&#8217;s all you need to know that it’s got a gorgeous, useful, and intuitive UI.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The headline explains what the app is in simple terms. (That&#8217;s fine, but it might be worth testing a benefit-oriented headline. Something like, &#8220;Scaling white-label design services just got a whole lot easier.&#8221;)&#160;Finally, there are no menu items on this registration page. Just a single call-to-action, and it only wants your email address. Keeping the ask small makes it more likely that visitors will convert.</p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\"/>\n\n\n\n<h3>3. Flyhomes gets their signup forms to pop up.</h3>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><a class=\"fancybox iframelpexamples\" href=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/flyhomes-full-signup-pages.png\" target=\"_blank\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/FlyHomes-Above-the-fold-Example-of-Signup-Form-Popup.gif\" alt=\"Animation of Flyhomes signup flow\" class=\"wp-image-97353\" width=\"1256\" height=\"603\"></a><figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">Image courtesy of <a href=\"https://www.flyhomes.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Flyhomes</a>. (Click to see the whole thing.)</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.flyhomes.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Flyhomes</a> makes buying and selling your homes easy, and profitable. (Their website copy is a fun read as well.)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Mm mm mm! If there&#8217;s one thing that&#8217;ll make me do a double-take, which is a super weird thing to do by yourself, it&#8217;s a remarkable form. (No, seriously.)&#160;Just look at that CTA: Start Now. There&#8217;s not a misleading word in there. (For example, it&#8217;s not, &#8220;Sign up now,&#8221; which wouldn&#8217;t be quite true.) And when you click on it, you&#8217;re prompted with, &#8220;Let&#8217;s Get Started.&#8221; </p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>Everything fades into the background when you click.</strong> All you need to do to get started is to give Flyhomes your email and whisper the sweet words every marketer wants to hear: &#8220;Nurture me.&#8221;</p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\"/>\n\n\n\n<h3>4. PointsBet delivers an irresistible offer.</h3>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/PointsBet-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example.png\" alt=\"An example of simple signup pages\" class=\"wp-image-97354\" width=\"1276\" https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/PointsBet-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-1536x683.png 1536w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/PointsBet-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-1000x445.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/PointsBet-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-650x289.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/PointsBet-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-300x133.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/PointsBet-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-160x71.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1276px) 100vw, 1276px\" /><figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">Image courtesy of <a href=\"https://www.zellermedia.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Zeller Media</a>.</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p><a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://pointsbet.com/\" target=\"_blank\">PointsBet</a> is an online bookmaker for sports and entertainment, based out of New Jersey.&#160;Props to <a href=\"https://www.zellermedia.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Zeller Media</a> for putting this one together. The agency did a fantastic job creating this signup page.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>This example shows that you don&#8217;t need a long-form landing page to convince prospects to convert. Think about this for a moment. Not only is this registration page asking you to sign up, but it&#8217;s also straight-up telling you that you need to make a $10 commitment.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>So how do you do that without scaring off your target audience? Offer them 10 times the amount back. Literally.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Veteran copywriter Roy Furr calls this <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.breakthroughmarketingsecrets.com/blog/how-to-create-an-irresistible-offer-example/\" target=\"_blank\">the irresistible offer</a>. Even a non-gambler can see the appeal. And for a gambler? It&#8217;s a no-brainer. Slip me an easy $10, which is peanuts, and you get $100 back. That&#8217;s a $90 profit! I&#8217;m no math scientist, but that&#8217;s a hell of a deal.</p>\n\n\n<div class=\"curated-tip\">\n    <div class=\"container inner text-left\">\n        <p><strong>Grow your agency with landing pages.</strong> Find out how Unbounce can help you <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/solutions/industry/agencies/\" target=_blank>win more conversions for your clients</a> and extend your menu of services using landing pages—no coding required.</p>\n    </div>\n</div>\n\n\n<h3>5. Heymarket double-dips with its call-to-action.</h3>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><a class=\"fancybox iframelpexamples\" href=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/heymarket-full-signup.png\" target=\"_blank\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/HeyMarket-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example.png\" alt=\"Screenshot of Heymarket page\" class=\"wp-image-97355\" width=\"1259\" height=\"669\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/HeyMarket-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example.png 2517w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/HeyMarket-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-150x80.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/HeyMarket-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-470x250.png 470w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/HeyMarket-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-80x43.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/HeyMarket-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-768x408.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/HeyMarket-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-1536x817.png 1536w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/HeyMarket-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-2048x1089.png 2048w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/HeyMarket-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-1000x532.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/HeyMarket-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-650x346.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/HeyMarket-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-300x159.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/HeyMarket-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-160x85.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1259px) 100vw, 1259px\" /></a><figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">Image courtesy of <a href=\"https://www.heymarket.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Heymarket</a>. (Click to see the whole thing.)</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.heymarket.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Heymarket</a> is a powerful SaaS platform that lets teams collaborate in business text messaging with customers.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>I like the headline in gray (&#8220;It&#8217;s not personal, it&#8217;s business&#8221;). It takes a saying that a villain in a movie might say to someone they&#8217;ve screwed over, and turns it on its head. This <em>is </em>business. Then the page tells you what the product is and ties it directly to the benefit in the headline.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The body copy simply expands upon this line, before presenting the initial pricing.&#160;The image is also immediately recognizable as a SaaS design, so there’s no mistaking where you are when you land. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Though sometimes multiple CTAs spell trouble, the double-dip on the calls-to-action here is a nice touch. This landing page puts the primary CTA under the body copy and the secondary CTA on the top right, space traditionally reserved for the menu. What I love about this is that the primary CTA invites the target audience to view a demo first, while the top-right button instead prompts the target to hop right into a free trial.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>What I would test though is this type of design against variants with photos of people as well as copy. SaaS is getting competitive. It’s becoming an increasingly saturated market, one where visual branding will play a greater role.<strong> </strong>Beyond a single landing page, <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/landing-page-articles/what-is-ab-testing/\" target=\"_blank\">A/B testing</a> can provide useful insights into which direction you should be guiding your brand.</p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\"/>\n\n\n\n<h3>6. Zire gets account creation flow right.</h3>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Zire-Ads-Above-the-fold-Example-of-Signup-Page.gif\" alt=\"Animation showing UI on Zire page\" class=\"wp-image-97357\" width=\"1252\" height=\"522\"><figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">Image courtesy of <a href=\"https://zire.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Zire</a>.</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p><a href=\"https://zire.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Zire</a> is an advertising platform for musicians, and it&#8217;s thoroughly impressive in its ease of use.&#160;In terms of visual style, this signup page is my favourite. The branding is spot-on, and the button leads to a magical wonderland of awesome UI:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"alignleft size-full is-resized\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/ZIRE-Flow.gif\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-97358\" width=\"1277\" height=\"655\"/></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>If you&#8217;re already on a platform like Spotify, as soon as you put your name in, your name, song, or album will pop up as a suggestion. The actual flow is a lot smoother, and it&#8217;s a pleasant experience through and through. Zire did a fantastic job with every aspect of this.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Wait! (Cue the record scratch.) </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Are we missing something here? </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Right. They haven’t asked for my email <em>yet</em>. <strong>But I’m engaged with their services, and ready to convert.</strong> Now that&#8217;s slick.</p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\"/>\n\n\n\n<h3>7. But if you&#8217;re offering me a 60-day trial, I&#8217;m intrigued enough to want to read through the copy and find out what I&#8217;m getting into. (Still, it&#8217;d be worth testing a variant with trimmed copy or a shorter form.)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>My favorite thing about this page, though, is how they’ve managed to squeeze all this essential information into an easily digestible and clean landing page.&#160;The fine print under the CTA also does a good job of addressing common objections: when they offer a 60-day free trial with no commitment, the company means business.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Free-trial pages have been around since modems used to screech at you. This signup landing page is a solid example showing that the underlying principles behind high-converting landing pages have changed little since the good ole&#8217; days.</p>\n\n\n\n<hr If the eye drifts up to their menu, they see a succinct description of the software instead. It&#8217;s a small thing, but it helps keep visitors focused.</p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\"/>\n\n\n\n<h3>9. Nakisa stays true to its messaging by staying organized.</h3>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><a class=\"fancybox iframelpexamples\" href=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/nakisa-full-signup-page.png\" target=\"_blank\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Nakisa-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example.png\" alt=\"Landing page by Nakisa\" class=\"wp-image-97362\" width=\"1157\" height=\"641\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Nakisa-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example.png 2314w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Nakisa-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-150x83.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Nakisa-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-452x250.png 452w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Nakisa-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-80x44.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Nakisa-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-768x425.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Nakisa-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-1536x850.png 1536w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Nakisa-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-2048x1134.png 2048w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Nakisa-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-1000x554.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Nakisa-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-650x360.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Nakisa-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-300x166.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Nakisa-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example-160x89.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1157px) 100vw, 1157px\" /></a><figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">Image courtesy of <a href=\"https://www.nakisa.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Nakisa</a>. (Click to see the whole thing.)</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.nakisa.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Nakisa</a> helps companies visualize their organizational structure so that they can make better business decisions.&#160;On this signup page, Nakisa makes the wins for its prospects easy to understand, specific, and tangible.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>This type of landing page can work well for SaaS B2B, in particular, for a couple of reasons: first, a B2B visitor is ready to buy because they&#8217;re actively shopping around for a solution. But the<strong> buyer journey isn&#8217;t linear because the B2B buyer tends to be research-savvy. </strong>They jump back and forth between the interest and consideration stages, and the consideration stage is much longer.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Second, B2B buyers also more interested in technical features than emotional appeals compared to B2C. That&#8217;s because they want to know all about the <strong>performance</strong> and <strong>return on their investment.</strong></p>\n\n\n\n<p>Nakisa understands this. For this target audience, the copy is direct and appealing to B2B buyers. The landing page includes a visually compelling clip of organizational design that shows how their software works. And the 14-day free trial offer lowers the barrier to test driving the product.</p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\"/>\n\n\n\n<h3>10. Targetable uses a testimonial to lure prospects in.</h3>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><a class=\"fancybox iframelpexamples\" href=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/targetable-full-signup-page.png\" target=\"_blank\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Targetable-Signup-Page-Example.png\" alt=\"Targetable sign up pages with testimonials\" class=\"wp-image-97363\" width=\"1189\" height=\"909\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Targetable-Signup-Page-Example.png 2378w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Targetable-Signup-Page-Example-150x115.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Targetable-Signup-Page-Example-327x250.png 327w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Targetable-Signup-Page-Example-80x61.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Targetable-Signup-Page-Example-768x587.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Targetable-Signup-Page-Example-1536x1174.png 1536w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Targetable-Signup-Page-Example-2048x1565.png 2048w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Targetable-Signup-Page-Example-1000x764.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Targetable-Signup-Page-Example-650x497.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Targetable-Signup-Page-Example-300x229.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Targetable-Signup-Page-Example-160x122.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1189px) 100vw, 1189px\" /></a><figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">Image courtesy of <a href=\"https://www.targetable.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Targetable</a>. (Click to see the whole thing.)</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.targetable.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Targetable</a> is an advertising platform that uses AI to help restaurants make more money with data.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Look at the quote they use as a heading on this signup page. Are there many restaurant owners who believe their restaurant is &#8220;amazing&#8221;? Sure. But this quote isn&#8217;t functioning as a testimonial, per se. Instead, the bottom subheading (in red, which helps it stand out) asks if you share this <strong>common sentiment</strong>. Then it presents <strong>a list of benefits that address this pain point, with a simple visual showcasing a platform feature.&#160;</strong></p>\n\n\n\n<p>This page is an excellent example of using creativity to vary your copy, while pushing the boundaries. (It&#8217;s also a great opportunity to A/B test the different ways you can present a pain point.)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Here, they&#8217;ve gone with a quote, but maybe something more direct would be more effective? Or perhaps a touch of humour would work? And some audiences could respond better to one headline, while others respond better to another. (A/B testing or using a tool like <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/product/smart-traffic-ppc/\">Smart Traffic</a> can help you find out what copy works best for winning new signups.)</p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\"/>\n\n\n\n<h3>11. Marley Spoon breaks the rules of signup pages, but smartly.</h3>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><a class=\"fancybox iframelpexamples\" class=\"wp-image-97364\" width=\"1239\" height=\"617\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Marley-Spoon-Signup-Page-Above-the-Fold-Example.png 2477w, Nom, nom, nom. This signup page does a couple of things extremely well.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>Like including a menu. (!) </strong><em>I know, I know.</em> Earlier, I noted that excluding the menu is the obvious move. (It&#8217;s certainly a landing page best practice.) But this menu here works, and here&#8217;s why I think it does: since Marley Spoon is a food subscription service, they provide a chance to look at the menu before taking advantage of the coupon. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>The other thing it does well?&#160;<strong>Those buttons are in different colors.&#160;</strong></p>\n\n\n\n<p>You know, even without reading the call to action, that these two buttons have two separate appeals. One’s a simple signup button, whereas the main CTA is a clear benefit-driven one: Save $80 in 4 weeks.&#160;That&#8217;s a strong 1-2 copy punch combo. Achieve <em>X </em>in <em>Y </em>amount of time.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"alignleft size-full is-resized\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Marley-Spoon-Signup-Steps.png\" alt=\"A detail from Marley Spoon's signup page\" class=\"wp-image-97365\" width=\"781\" height=\"991\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Marley-Spoon-Signup-Steps.png 1562w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Marley-Spoon-Signup-Steps-118x150.png 118w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Marley-Spoon-Signup-Steps-197x250.png 197w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Marley-Spoon-Signup-Steps-63x80.png 63w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Marley-Spoon-Signup-Steps-768x975.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Marley-Spoon-Signup-Steps-1211x1536.png 1211w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Marley-Spoon-Signup-Steps-1000x1269.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Marley-Spoon-Signup-Steps-650x825.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Marley-Spoon-Signup-Steps-300x381.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Marley-Spoon-Signup-Steps-126x160.png 126w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 781px) 100vw, 781px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>And would you look at that beautiful account creation flow?&#160;The steps are numbered <em>and </em>labeled, clearly managing visitor expectations every step of the way. All the visitor is required to do is click away at the options as they reach the last leg of the race (indicated in glowing gold!). <strong>Talk about giving the visitor a sense of satisfaction.</strong></p>\n\n\n\n<p>They make getting all that food delivered right to your doorstep to look effortless. (And tasty too.) Mwah! A chef&#8217;s kiss.</p>\n\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\"/>\n\n\n\n<h3>12. If you need a way to manage your visual assets, then you just can’t say no to Libris, and this landing page shows you why.&#160;</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Let&#8217;s end this list of examples with Libris&#8217; no-brainer offer, which ticks all the boxes:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>60-day trial? Check.</li><li>Body copy explaining how Libris can make life a little easier for your marketing team? Check.</li><li>Two different-colored buttons hinting at different purposes? Check.&#160;</li><li>Awesome aerial shot of a beach with very few people to line this up with the “exclusive” feel and mention in the headline? Check.</li><li>A badge showcasing a super-recent award as a Top 100 software company from G2? Amazing!</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>If you&#8217;ve got it, flaunt it, especially if you&#8217;ve received a significant award and recognition from an industry leader in your space. The award from G2 is a <strong>major trust booster</strong> and signals indirectly to your visitors that they&#8217;re missing out if they don&#8217;t try Libris out. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>One thing I would test is the &#8220;limited time offer&#8221; message. When something&#8217;s limited, you should indicate the period or the deadline. Don&#8217;t do it, and your message can feel somewhat generic and fall flat. Do it, and make your target audience perceive and <em>feel </em>the scarcity.&#160;Feeling inspired yet? ","https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/blog-visual-cta-2x-v2.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn23@2020_3/2020/08/25/00-36-01-122_e094db9e1b450484.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598315757679},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 08:35:57","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 08:35:57","title":"How to Build Your Brand with Landing Page Optimization","link":"https://unbounce.com/?p=97707","description":"<p>Let’s face it:<em> brand marketers get a bad rap</em>. In the last decade, the conversation has focused on technical marketing: growth hacking, conversion rate optimization, SEO, the merging of product and marketing, and data, data, data. At the same time, brand became less exciting—and sometimes an afterthought. It was too “fluffy.”</p> \n<p>But that’s all changing. Companies have found their edge by investing in incredible brands, and <strong>a company’s brand has become its differentiator</strong>. Look to <a href=\"https://www.theverge.com/2020/6/15/21286466/hey-email-basecamp-price-availability-platforms-launch\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">the recent launch of Hey</a> or other companies like Equal Parts, Headspace, Warby Parker, Casper, and Notion as examples.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>It might seem like building a brand doesn’t line up with the idea of being&nbsp;data-driven. But we<strong> can apply what we’ve learned about technical marketing over the last decade to build better brands</strong> and make better decisions in today’s data-driven world.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Through customer research, landing page testing, conversion rate optimization, and traditional brand development tactics, you can be smarter about building and evolving your brand. Landing page optimization can serve as your testing ground for this stuff, and I’ll show you how.</p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"alignleft size-large is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/blue-rectangle-horizontal.svg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-93558\" width=\"25\" height=\"5\" />\n </figure>\n</div> \n<h2><strong>What Goes Into a Brand?</strong></h2> \n<p>Before we dive into how to take a data-driven approach to building a brand, let’s make sure we are on the same page about what <em>makes up</em> a brand. The short answer is “a lot.” But for this overview, I’ll focus on a few critical parts:</p> \n<ul>\n <li>The look and feel (design, user experience)</li>\n <li>The voice, tone, and messaging</li>\n <li>The positioning (versus others in the market)</li>\n <li>The overall brand promise</li>\n</ul> \n<p>The <strong>look and feel</strong> of a tech brand is mostly encapsulated in the design, feel, and user experience (UX) of both the website and product. Everything (from a company’s <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.canva.com/colors/color-wheel/\" target=\"_blank\">color scheme</a> to the feel of its animations) matters when trying to convey a personality. Look to <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://design.studio/work/airbnb\" target=\"_blank\">Airbnb</a> as an example of how important the design and feel can be in establishing your brand’s personality:</p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-airbnb.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-97737\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-airbnb.png 1054w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-airbnb-150x150.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-airbnb-251x250.png 251w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-airbnb-80x80.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-airbnb-768x765.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-airbnb-1000x996.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-airbnb-650x648.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-airbnb-300x299.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-airbnb-160x160.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1054px) 100vw, 1054px\" />\n  <figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">\n   Here you can see Airbnb’s visuals convey feelings of fun, diversity, and being human. The colors also express a sort of playful yet modern feeling.\n  </figcaption>\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>The <strong>voice, tone, and messaging</strong> of a company make up the “written words” of the brand. Pretty straightforward, but it’s important to note that companies should aim to <strong>make this attractive to the right person at the right time </strong>(and that’s where landing page testing can come in).&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Your company’s <strong>positioning in-market versus your competitors</strong> is an essential part of your brand. How do you distinguish yourself against the alternatives? Why should someone choose YOU over THEM? You only have so much real estate. What you want to say can vary depending on a variety of factors, like your personas and where they are in the funnel (i.e., people who are just discovering you versus ready to make a purchase).</p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-figma.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-97740\" width=\"1440\" height=\"672\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-figma.png 1920w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-figma-150x70.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-figma-536x250.png 536w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-figma-80x37.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-figma-768x358.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-figma-1536x717.png 1536w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-figma-1000x467.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-figma-650x303.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-figma-300x140.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-figma-160x75.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1440px) 100vw, 1440px\" />\n  <figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">\n   Figma positioned versus a competitor.\n  </figcaption>\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>Finally, the overall <strong>brand promise</strong> represents what you are promising to deliver to your customers. What is that <em>thing </em>you are promising? Sometimes it can be something as straightforward as a promise in your tagline: “15 minutes could save you 15% or more on car insurance.” It’s important to balance:&nbsp;</p> \n<ol>\n <li>how you position yourself against competitors;</li>\n <li>what is attractive to your target customers;</li>\n <li>and what you can deliver on.</li>\n</ol> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-geico.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-97741\" width=\"600\" height=\"350\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-geico.png 1200w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-geico-150x88.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-geico-429x250.png 429w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-geico-80x47.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-geico-768x448.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-geico-1000x583.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-geico-650x379.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-geico-300x175.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-geico-160x93.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px\" />\n  <figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">\n   Geico delivers its brand promise in a tagline.\n  </figcaption>\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>Your messaging and positioning will differ significantly based on these factors above. <strong>How your product serves one <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/landing-pages/scientific-model-for-emotionally-powerful-landing-pages/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><strong>persona</strong></a> may be far different than how it serves another.</strong></p> \n<p>A solid understanding of all of this will result in a successful marketing team and (likely) company growth. But this is also what most marketing and product teams mess up. Without the data, people tend to make assumptions. Or marketers aren’t customer-centric enough in their approach, and they deliver the wrong message, brand, or feel to the wrong person at the wrong time.</p> \n<p>The great thing about all of this is that <strong>we can use landing page testing and conversion rate optimization to test and validate all of these elements of your brand</strong>. Let’s explore a few ways you can get this done (fast).</p> \n<h2>1. Use landing page testing to validate your personas.</h2> \n<p>Say you are revisiting your target customers and why they decide to use your product. Understanding what resonates with each persona at each stage may be hard to figure out. It usually takes a lot of research, but you can also get quicker answers with landing pages.</p> \n<p>Below are a few examples of how you can do this. For these tests, it’s best to send traffic to these landing pages with an <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/landing-page-articles/what-is-ab-testing/\" target=\"_blank\">A/B test</a> (which you can do in Unbounce). You can drive traffic to the pages using paid ads on Facebook, for instance, or you can tap into your existing audiences and push traffic via email—in either case, split the traffic for reliable comparisons.</p> \n<h3>Test different calls to action to let users self identify.</h3> \n<p>On your landing page, create the isolated options that someone can click to self-identify. For example, describe your product for specific personas and with clear self-identifying calls to action (e.g., “I’m a marketer”). See the example below:</p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-97745\" width=\"1917\" height=\"894\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example.png 1917w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-150x70.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-536x250.png 536w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-80x37.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-768x358.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-1536x716.png 1536w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-1000x466.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-650x303.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-300x140.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-160x75.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1917px) 100vw, 1917px\" />\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>From there, push them into the funnel or purchase page and see which CTAs get the most clicks and have the best conversion rates. You can use this data to see which audience your product resonates with most and validate or invalidate specific personas.</p> \n<h3>Test different jobs-to-be-done through CTA optimization.</h3> \n<p>To gather data around which jobs your users are hiring you to do, test different CTAs with those audiences. Allow them to self-select, just like in the example above. But here we put different <a href=\"https://jtbd.info/2-what-is-jobs-to-be-done-jtbd-796b82081cca\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">jobs to be done</a> side-by-side with our product. <strong>With this data, you can see the most common and attractive use cases for your product.</strong>&nbsp;</p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-2.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-97746\" width=\"1914\" height=\"856\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-2.png 1914w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-2-150x67.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-2-560x250.png 560w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-2-80x36.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-2-768x343.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-2-1536x687.png 1536w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-2-1000x447.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-2-650x291.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-2-300x134.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-2-160x72.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1914px) 100vw, 1914px\" />\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>You can also run different landing pages entirely and see which one converts best in an A/B test.&nbsp;These are not going to give teams definitive answers about your personas and why they use your product, but they’ll inform those strategic discussions. And it’s far better than going into this strategy blind. </p> \n<p>\n <div>\n  By running ads or segmented campaigns via email and pushing those users to landing pages with messaging or design that you seek to test, \n  <strong>you can stop guessing and learn more quickly.</strong>\n </div></p> \n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\" /> \n<h2>2. Use conversion rate optimization (CRO) to improve your positioning.</h2> \n<p>Landing pages are also the perfect way to <strong>test your product’s positioning with consumers. </strong>One of the best things you can do via landing page optimization is test your positioning against competitors.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>How? Run an A/B test of a page showing you versus your competitors and have different positioning/messaging on each variant. See which one wins by looking at traffic, CTRs, and conversion rates. (Be careful here: a best practice is to avoid direct side-by-side comparisons against your competitors.)</p> \n<p>Look to this Zendesk example below for inspiration:</p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/zendesk-vs-desk.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-97751\" width=\"960\" height=\"1350\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/zendesk-vs-desk.png 1920w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/zendesk-vs-desk-107x150.png 107w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/zendesk-vs-desk-178x250.png 178w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/zendesk-vs-desk-57x80.png 57w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/zendesk-vs-desk-768x1080.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/zendesk-vs-desk-1092x1536.png 1092w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/zendesk-vs-desk-1456x2048.png 1456w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/zendesk-vs-desk-1000x1406.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/zendesk-vs-desk-650x914.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/zendesk-vs-desk-300x422.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/zendesk-vs-desk-114x160.png 114w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 960px) 100vw, 960px\" />\n  <figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">\n   (Source: \n   <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.zendesk.com/zendesk-vs-desk/\" target=\"_blank\">Zendesk</a> via \n   <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.crayon.co/blog/great-competitive-comparison-pages\" target=\"_blank\">Crayon</a>)\n  </figcaption>\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>You can also refine other parts of your positioning within your landing pages. For example, you can test headline copy with particular personas to see which positioning of your product resonates better with each.&nbsp;Or, as you push traffic at different funnel stages to landing pages, you can learn when to include a “learn more” versus “buy now” call to action. Testing CTAs will help you better understand what customers want at different parts of the user journey.</p> \n<p>Finally, any ongoing testing will likely involve <strong>the refinement of your <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/conversion-glossary/definition/unique-value-proposition/\" target=\"_blank\"><strong>core value prop</strong></a> and product positioning.</strong> As you gather data from landing page performance and change the copy and design, note what wins. And, as you discover more winners, share this data with those in charge of your overall product positioning. Based on these opportunities, they can make improvements to the messaging and framing of the product against competitors.&nbsp;</p> \n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\" /> \n<h2>3. Using CRO to find the best brand promise.</h2> \n<p>This may be the most straightforward thing you can do with landing page testing. How? Test and validate your main value prop in your landing page headline. Here’s one approach I have taken when trying to validate our best headlines:</p> \n<ol>\n <li>Develop your top <strong>2-5 headlines</strong> based on your brand factors (personas, position in market, product value, etc.)</li>\n <li>Create a short landing page with the same sections below it and the same CTA (e.g., “Learn More”).</li>\n <li>Create variants of the page with each headline you’ve devised.</li>\n <li>See which one gets the most clicks/leads/sign-ups/purchases.</li>\n</ol> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-3.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-97747\" width=\"1920\" height=\"746\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-3.png 1920w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-3-150x58.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-3-560x218.png 560w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-3-80x31.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-3-768x298.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-3-1536x597.png 1536w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-3-1000x389.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-3-650x253.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-3-300x117.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/brand-example-3-160x62.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1920px) 100vw, 1920px\" />\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>With this, you should start gathering data on CTRs that resonate best and you will have <strong>data that is more valuable than a simple survey</strong>:&nbsp;which copy <em>actually</em> got people to convert?</p> \n<div class=\"blog-cta-image-section\" data-ga=\"\">\n <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/?p=97707/unbounce.com/product/features/unlimited-ab-testing/\" target=\"_blank\" data-campaign=\"\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/2.5_VisualCTA_AB.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"2260\" height=\"1217\" /></a>\n</div> \n<h2>4. Ease tension between technical and brand marketing teams.</h2> \n<p>There’s always an inherent tension between the teams focused on conversion and those focused on brand. Conversion-oriented marketing teams push the boundaries of the brand to drive sign-ups, purchases, and more. Brand teams seek to rein in this approach to avoid going “off-brand.”&nbsp;</p> \n<p><strong>Data-driven approaches to brand development can smooth out this tension.</strong> </p> \n<p>The conversion-focused marketing team can build relationships with brand teams by proactively testing messages, designs, and positioning through landing pages. (Brand teams might not know these things are possible.)&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Plus, you can use landing pages to push the boundaries of the brand. Test the “off-brand” stuff by running small scale tests for copy, positioning, and design. The company faces less risk that way, but it may gain some interesting insights that help inform your strategy.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Build alignment by testing things together and evolving the brand <em>together</em>.&nbsp;</p> \n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\" /> \n<h2>Key considerations when using data to inform your brand strategy.</h2> \n<p>When using A/B testing to iterate on your brand, there are some key things to note. More than anything, the team must <strong>avoid making decisions using biased data. </strong>Data is only as useful as its source. </p> \n<p>Audiences are your most important consideration here:</p> \n<ul>\n <li>Who are you sending to these landing pages?&nbsp;</li>\n <li>What’s their context?&nbsp;</li>\n</ul> \n<p>Careful consideration of these two questions can make or break any data that comes from landing page testing.&nbsp;In general, you should <strong>align your ad with your landing page</strong> as much as possible to avoid confusing the visitor.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Here are some other things to think about when evaluating the validity of your landing page tests:</p> \n<ul>\n <li><strong>How confident are you that an up-funnel optimization will not lead to adverse behavior down the funnel?</strong> Or, said more simply, is your messaging <em>deceptive</em>? Use your best judgment here and ensure you tie landing page performance to down-funnel metrics.</li>\n <li><strong>Are you trying to get in front of new people or existing people?</strong> People who know your brand or don’t? Identify the best audiences and find them—push people via email or ads or serve up the landing page(s) in a survey. Choose the right audience based on what answer you are trying to get. Similar to choosing the right audience for research, choose the right audience for landing page testing.</li>\n <li>If possible,<strong> segment the traffic to your landing pages to narrow down what is working for whom.</strong> For example, if your company serves both engineers and designers, separate the ads and landing pages for these audiences so you can understand what works for each audience independently.</li>\n</ul> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"alignleft size-large\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/pink-rectangle-horizontal.svg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-93559\" />\n </figure>\n</div> \n<h2><strong>Tying It All Together</strong></h2> \n<p>Everything I’ve described here is really just a derivative of research, but you are testing it in a more robust and informative way. <strong>By giving people more context and a “real” feel via landing pages, you’ll get better answers to the most pressing questions about your brand.</strong>&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Brand and data-driven marketing don’t need to be separate. By working together, conversion rate optimization pros can inform brand strategies and help companies better understand their customers’ desires, needs, and values.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Try a completely different approach to how you position yourself or even test landing pages against your traditional product positioning. See what sticks and see if you can refine how you speak to your customers across the board. If that doesn’t work, roll things back and try it again. You can evolve your brand over time, but this is a great way to start.</p> \n<div class=\"blog-cta-image-section\" data-ga=\"\">\n <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/product/smart-traffic/\" target=\"_blank\" data-campaign=\"\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/smart-traffic-blog-visual-cta.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"2260\" height=\"1216\" /></a>\n</div>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Tue, 21 Jul 2020 07:01:00
