598315757677},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 08:35:57","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 08:35:57","title":"How to Do a Webinar That’s as Exciting as an In-Person Event","link":"https://unbounce.com/?p=97196","description":"<p>There’s something special about attending an in-person conference or industry event. The adrenaline rush of going to pick up your nametag on the first day. The opening keynote that gets everyone in the room buzzing. The networking breaks where you awkwardly introduce yourself to strangers and mingle over tiny sandwiches. (OK, maybe that’s just me.)</p> \n<p>This year though, almost every single conference and event has been either delayed or canceled. COVID-19 has put a pause on large group gatherings of all kinds, and many event organizers have been left scrambling to figure out what they can or should do as an alternative.</p> \n<p>One option is to take your event online and run a webinar (or perhaps, a series of webinars), instead. But can you really replicate all that buzz, networking, and opportunity over a laptop screen? How can you possibly do a webinar that’s as exciting as an in-person event?</p> \n<p><strong>Charlene Ditch, Founder and CEO of </strong><a href=\"https://charlenekateevents.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><strong>Charlene Kate Events</strong></a>, says the potential is there for marketers who are prepared to put in the effort:</p> \n<div class=\"blog-photo\">\n <img class=\"alignright size-full wp-image-96860\" src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Charlene-Quote.png\" alt=\"Charlene Ditch, Founder and CEO of Charlene Kate Events\" width=\"83\" height=\"83\" />\n</div> \n<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote\">\n <p><em>We’re navigating a new world and while we must adapt, we still have to be thoughtful in how we deliver the attendee experience. It’s an exciting time to be an event marketer and I’m confident that if we are strategic and intentional about the way we message, market, and execute—we can deliver something magical.”</em></p>\n</blockquote> \n<p>Here at Unbounce, we know from experience that Charlene speaks the truth. Our team has years of experience running everything from large-scale, in-person conferences (you can get your tickets to <a href=\"https://calltoactionconference.unbounce.com/\">CTAConf21 right here</a>) to smaller-scale virtual events (like <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/marketing-optimization-week/\" target=\"_blank\">Marketing Optimization Week</a>). We’ve learned a lot along the way about what works online—and what really doesn’t.</p> \n<p>So to help you out, we put together this guide to make your first experience organizing a webinar way less awkward, and way more awesome. Find out how to pick the right speakers, get set up with the best tools, and make it <em>genuinely</em> exciting for attendees to participate.</p> \n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\" /> \n<h2>How to Run a Webinar or Virtual Event Like a Pro</h2> \n<ol>\n <li><a href=\"https://unbounce.com/?p=97196#Tip1\">Align Your Theme and Dates</a></li>\n <li><a href=\"https://unbounce.com/?p=97196#Tip2\">Track Your Webinar Goals</a></li>\n <li><a href=\"https://unbounce.com/?p=97196#Tip3\">Recruit a Lineup of Star Speakers</a></li>\n <li><a href=\"https://unbounce.com/?p=97196#Tip4\">Set Up Your Webinar Platform and Tools</a></li>\n <li><a href=\"https://unbounce.com/?p=97196#Tip5\">Promote the Event to Create Buzz</a></li>\n <li><a href=\"https://unbounce.com/?p=97196#Tip6\">Perform Dry-Runs</a></li>\n <li><a href=\"https://unbounce.com/?p=97196#Tip7\">Make Magic Happen on the Day</a></li>\n <li><a href=\"https://unbounce.com/?p=97196#Tip8\">Follow Through Post-Event</a></li>\n</ol> \n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\" /> \n<h2 id=\"Tip1\">1. Align Your Theme and Dates</h2> \n<p>Every great online event starts with a great idea. You want to put something out there that nobody else has ever done before (or do it better than anyone else)—and this can be challenging when there are hundreds of webinars happening every single month.</p> \n<p>That’s why the theme you choose is so important. You want to <strong>cover a topic that your audience truly cares about</strong> and <strong>find a unique angle they can’t resist</strong>. You’ll want to brainstorm ways you can incorporate this theme into each of your speaker topics, the visual identity of your event, and the actual takeaways that attendees will be talking about afterward.</p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Digtal-Agency-Day.png\" alt=\"A webinar example by Unbounce: Digital Agency Day\" class=\"wp-image-96526\" width=\"960\" height=\"488\">\n   <figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">\n    The theme for \n    <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://digitalagencyday.com/\">Digital Agency Day</a> was growth—how agencies can scale up with tactics from the top experts in their industry. \n   </figcaption></img>\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>So how do you choose the theme for your virtual event? Here are some things to consider…</p> \n<ul>\n <li><strong>Does it relate to a problem your target audience is trying to solve? </strong>Always approach your webinar from a customer-first perspective. Look for pain points that they care about, goals they’re trying to achieve, and opportunities they would like to pursue. Test out your theme by asking your current customers if they’d be interested in the topic.</li>\n <li><strong>Do you have expertise in this space?</strong> In order to attract qualified leads, the theme of your event should relate back to your business. Nobody wants to attend a pet grooming webinar put on by McDonald’s, for example. (Although I do wonder how they always manage to perfectly style the fur on <a href=\"https://mcdonalds.fandom.com/wiki/Grimace\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Grimace</a>.)</li>\n <li><strong>Are there industry experts who can speak on this theme?</strong> You might get stuck if the theme you choose is too narrow or niche. Ideally, there should be a few experts who can speak on this theme or other companies that you can imagine wanting to partner up for the event.</li>\n</ul> \n<p>It also helps if you can tie your webinar to real-world events that are happening in your industry, or other important dates on the calendar. For example, right now many companies are putting on special webinar series to help their customers adapt to COVID-19.</p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Keela-Webinar.png\" alt=\"A Virtual Event by Keela\" class=\"wp-image-96526\" width=\"960\" height=\"488\">\n   <figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">\n    This webinar series was put on by \n    <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.keela.co/lp/adaptation-series\">Keela</a> to help non-profit organizations adapt to COVID-19. \n   </figcaption></img>\n </figure>\n</div> \n<h2 id=\"Tip2\">2. Track Your Webinar Goals</h2> \n<p>Webinars are an excellent opportunity to generate leads for your business and <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/campaign-strategy/how-to-build-an-email-list/\">build up your email list</a>. Depending on the topic you choose and how heavily you promote the event, this will be an opportunity to reach new leads and get them interacting with your brand for the very first time. That’s why it helps to set a few goals at the start so you can be strategic with your planning and track how much ROI you drive from your efforts.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Here are some of the most important goals you should think about earl on:</p> \n<ul>\n <li><strong>Number of Registrants</strong> – Set a realistic goal for the number of registrants you’re hoping will sign up for your webinar. It’s OK if this number changes as you start building out your event—the actual number of registrants will depend on your promo efforts, your partnerships, and how much traffic you drive to the sign-up page.</li>\n <li><strong>Number of Attendees </strong>– According to the latest <a href=\"https://www.on24.com/resources/assets/report-webinar-benchmarks-2019/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">webinar benchmarks from On24</a>, an average of 56% of registrants show up to attend an online event. This number drops to 43% if you’re expecting more than 100 attendees—so be realistic, and expect only about half of your registrants to actually be there on the day.</li>\n <li><strong>Number of Sales or Sign-Ups</strong> – The final goal you’ll want to track is how many registrants or attendees end up becoming customers with your business afterward. You can set a projected goal for this based on your business model and the types of leads you plan to attract.</li>\n</ul> \n<h2 id=\"Tip3\">3. Recruit a Lineup of Star Speakers</h2> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/MOW-Speakers.png\" alt=\"Recruit High-Profile Speakers for Your Webinar\" class=\"wp-image-96526\" width=\"960\" height=\"488\">\n   <figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">\n    For \n    <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/marketing-optimization-week/\">Marketing Optimization Week</a>, the Unbounce team recruited high-profile names and reps from high-profile companies to speak at the event.\n   </figcaption></img>\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>This is a big one. Because the first thing anyone does when they see a new webinar or online event is to check who’s going to be speaking. If you don’t have the right name recognition or expertise on deck, then a lot of people just aren’t going to be all that interested.</p> \n<p><strong>Rachel Scott, Senior Marketing Manager at Unbounce</strong>, says that there are three valuable things to look for when creating your ideal list of speakers:</p> \n<div class=\"blog-photo\">\n <img class=\"alignright size-full wp-image-96860\" src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Rachel-Quote.png\" alt=\"Rachel Scott, Senior Marketing Manager at Unbounce\" width=\"83\" height=\"83\" />\n</div> \n<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote\">\n <p>Recognizable names are a huge draw, so you’ll want to look for those first. But there are also company names that can be just as important. Try to find a balance between the two, while also actively searching for diversity and different points of view. Check out other industry webinars and see who has been speaking recently—you can find a lot of great presenters that way, and they’ll probably be more keen to participate.</p>\n</blockquote> \n<p>You’ll want to start recruiting early because you need your speaker line-up in place before you can start promoting your event. One other tip that Rachel suggested is to offer a <strong>lead sharing opportunity</strong> to big-name partners or speakers who would help expand your reach.</p> \n<div class=\"blog-photo\">\n <img class=\"alignright size-full wp-image-96860\" src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Rachel-Quote.png\" alt=\"Rachel Scott, Senior Marketing Manager at Unbounce\" width=\"83\" height=\"83\" />\n</div> \n<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote\">\n <p>Give speakers and partners the opportunity to generate leads for their business as well. You could offer a one-to-one lead share for example, and for every lead they help bring into the webinar you’ll give them access to another lead who registered. That way, they have an incentive to drive registrations to the event and spread the word. Alternatively, you can set a registration goal for them, where if they bring in a certain number of leads you’ll share the full list of webinar registrations.</p>\n</blockquote> \n<p>In your pitch to speakers, you’ll want to emphasize <strong>what’s in it for them</strong>. Whether that’s lead sharing, a partnership opportunity for their company, the number of attendees they’ll be able to reach, or who they’ll be speaking alongside at the event.</p> \n<p><strong>Do You Need a Webinar Host?</strong></p> \n<p>A host or moderator can help make your online event more exciting and easy to follow for attendees. Look for someone within your own company who might be great at this task—charming, friendly, and knowledgeable. You can have them introduce each guest, run Q&amp;A sessions with speakers, and act as the “face” of the event to make it more personal.</p> \n<h2 id=\"Tip4\">4. Set Up Your Webinar Platform and Tools</h2> \n<p>There are a number of different platforms you can use to run your webinar or online event. Here are a few of the most popular options that <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/product/integrations/\">integrate with Unbounce</a> landing pages:</p> \n<ul>\n <li><a href=\"https://unbounce.com/product/integrations/zapier/?integration=gotowebinar\">GoToWebinar</a></li>\n <li><a href=\"https://zapier.com/apps/unbounce/integrations/demio\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Demio</a>&nbsp;</li>\n <li><a href=\"https://zapier.com/apps/unbounce/integrations/livestorm\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Livestorm</a></li>\n <li><a href=\"https://zapier.com/apps/unbounce/integrations/zoom\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Zoom</a></li>\n</ul> \n<p>Your choice will ultimately come down to the features you need, how much control you want over the platform, and what price point makes sense for your business.</p> \n<p>Beyond the webinar platform itself, you’ll also want to set up a landing page to promote the event and bring in new registrants. You can use Unbounce to quickly set up a page that highlights your speakers and encourages attendees to sign up. Check out our <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/landing-page-templates/event/\">event landing page templates</a> to get started, or see more <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/landing-page-examples/webinar-landing-page-examples/\">webinar landing page examples and best practices for 2020</a>.</p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Evento-Template.png\" alt=\"Landing Page Template for Virtual Events and Webinars\" class=\"wp-image-96526\" width=\"960\" height=\"488\">\n   <figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">\n    The \n    <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/landing-page-template/evento/\">Evento landing page template</a> would work perfectly for an online event or webinar series.\n   </figcaption></img>\n </figure>\n</div> \n<h2 id=\"Tip5\">5. Promote the Event to Create Buzz</h2> \n<p>Now that you’ve got your speakers on board and your registration landing page set up, it’s time to start promoting your webinar. You’ll want to build in at least <strong>one month of lead time</strong> for your promo efforts in order to give visitors enough chances to sign up.&nbsp;</p> \n<p><strong>Send Out Promo</strong> <strong>Emails</strong></p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Screen-Shot-2020-07-13-at-8.41.14-AM.png\" alt=\"A Webinar Promo Email Example\" class=\"wp-image-96526\" width=\"960\" height=\"488\">\n   <figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">\n    You can send out promo emails like this one to build anticipation for your webinar or online event.\n   </figcaption></img>\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>Here at Unbounce, we’ve found emails to be the single most effective way to promote webinars. Open rates and click-through rates tend to be higher here than any other channel.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Try to split out some segments of your list you think would be particularly interested in the subject matter, and send out <strong>a series of three</strong> <strong>promotional emails</strong> inviting them to attend.</p> \n<ul>\n <li><strong>Email One</strong> <strong>(“The Invitation Email”)</strong> – Send this one out about a month before your online event. This is the big unveiling of your event, so you’ll want to treat it with the right level of fanfare to get recipients excited. Focus on the customer-centric benefits of your theme, and the big reasons they’ll want to attend.</li>\n <li><strong>Email Two (“The Speaker Email”) </strong>– A week or two later, send a follow-up email that goes into a bit more detail about who will be speaking at the event. This is where you can do some name-dropping and get into more specifics about different topics on the agenda.</li>\n <li><strong>Email Three (“The Last Chance Email”) </strong>– This one should go out a day or two before the event, and really lean on the FOMO of your audience. It would be a shame if they missed out on this event that so many of their peers will be attending.</li>\n</ul> \n<p><strong>Build Anticipation on Social Media</strong></p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/MozCon-Twitter.png\" alt=\"How to Promote Your Online Event on Social Media\" class=\"wp-image-96526\" width=\"480\" height=\"244\">\n   <figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">\n    Use social media to raise awareness and get more attendees excited for your event.\n   </figcaption></img>\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>Posting about your event on Twitter, Facebook, and LinkedIn can help build buzz for your target audience and make them more likely to attend. That’s because <a href=\"https://thefinancialbrand.com/42323/advertising-marketing-messages-effective-frequency/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">the more times someone sees an ad, the more likely they will be to take action</a>. If it seems like everybody is talking about your webinar on social media, that will help convince some of these folks to get curious enough to attend.</p> \n<p>In the weeks leading up to the big day, try sprinkling in more and more posts about the event. Ramp up the frequency as you get closer to create more “buzz” on the timeline and encourage other attendees to post about it as well.</p> \n<p><strong>Ask Speakers to Promote Your Event</strong></p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Speaker-Promo.png\" alt=\"Speakers Can Help You Promote Your Webinar on Social Media\" class=\"wp-image-96526\" width=\"480\" height=\"244\">\n   <figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">\n    Ask speakers to promote your event to help bring in new audiences.\n   </figcaption></img>\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>Your speakers want the webinar to be as successful as possible too, because their name is attached to the event. So why not tap into their networks and ask them for help with promotion?</p> \n<p>This can be a great strategy to bring in new leads who you might not otherwise reach on your own. Because almost everybody has an audience—whether that’s through a blog, an email list, or on social media. And even a simple retweet from the right speaker could provide a significant attendance boost to your online event.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Make sure to ask speakers early on to get their buy-in, and consider offering some sort of lead share (as we talked about earlier) to give them even more of a promotional incentive. </p> \n<p><strong>Use Popups and Sticky Bars on Your Website</strong></p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Sticky-Bar-Template-Set-a-Reminder.png\" alt=\"The Set a Reminder Sticky Bar Template for Webinars\" class=\"wp-image-96526\" width=\"960\" height=\"488\">\n   <figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">\n    Use a sticky bar on your website to let visitors know about your virtual event.\n   </figcaption></img>\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>You can set up a <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/product/popups-and-sticky-bars/\">popup or sticky bar</a> to appear on your website and promote the event. This is a great way to turn any relevant or high-traffic page into a vehicle for getting visitors to your webinar registration page. You could even place one on your website homepage if you’re serious about driving more registrations.</p> \n<p>Personally, I’m a big fan of the <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/landing-page-template/set-a-reminder/\">Set a Reminder sticky bar template</a>—the ticking countdown clock gets the attention of folks scrolling, but it doesn’t intrude too much on the page itself.</p> \n<h2 id=\"Tip6\">6. Perform Dry-Runs</h2> \n<p>What’s the biggest thing that separates a ho-hum webinar from an amazing online experience? Practice. (Sorry—that’s like a way less funny version of the <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/2009/11/29/nyregion/29fyi.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">famous Carnegie Hall joke</a>.)</p> \n<p>Sure, you can put your faith in your speakers and just <em>hope</em> they do a great job on the big day. But if you want to elevate your virtual event and really make it seem polished for attendees like an in-person event, <strong>we would highly recommend doing a dry run with each speaker first</strong>.</p> \n<p>Set up times with all your speakers a week or two before the event, and ask them to go through their presentation as they would when they’re live. While they’re going through, you should look for opportunities and areas of improvement around…</p> \n<ul>\n <li><strong>Content Flow</strong> – Are they making clear points? Can you follow the flow of the presentation? Do they spend too long on one slide and not enough time somewhere else? Are there any holes or obvious questions they can address?</li>\n <li><strong>Delivery</strong> – Not everyone is a natural-born speaker. Look for opportunities to improve their delivery, and make recommendations based on how they perform the dry-run. If someone’s delivery seems off, you may want to ask them to continue practicing and schedule another dry-run before going live.</li>\n <li><strong>Visuals</strong> – To give your event a cohesive feel, try giving each speaker a slide deck template to use. Look for any style inconsistencies or visuals that could be improved during the dry-runs. (E.g., blurry photos, hard-to-read fonts, etc.) You should also check each speaker’s background to make sure the lighting is easy on the eyes, their microphone is clear, and their connection is stable. (For inspiration, check out some of the <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://moz.com/blog/behind-the-scenes-at-mozcon-virtual\" target=\"_blank\">behind-the-scenes equipment MozCon speakers are using</a> for their presentations this year. <em>Très fancy!</em>)</li>\n <li><strong>Technical Requirements</strong> – Do they need to play a video during their presentation? Is there a web link they want to show? Better to know about these ahead of time than to be surprised live on the day of the webinar.</li>\n</ul> \n<p>You’ll also want to do a run-through with your host, and make sure they know what they’ll be saying before and after each presentation. Go over the pronunciation of each speaker’s name, and hold a mock Q&amp;A session so they get a feel for how they’ll be able to interact with attendees.</p> \n<h2 id=\"Tip7\">7. Make Magic Happen on the Day</h2> \n<p>On the day of your webinar, you’ll want to go above and beyond to bring some of that in-person excitement to attendees. Here are a few of the things you can do to really put the “event” in your “virtual event.”</p> \n<p><strong>Make It Interactive</strong></p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Screen-Shot-2020-07-13-at-9.36.24-AM.png\" alt=\"MozCon is encouraging socialization and networking at their virtual event.\" class=\"wp-image-96526\" width=\"960\" height=\"488\">\n   <figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">\n    I love how \n    <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://moz.com/mozcon\">MozCon</a> is building in virtual networking time into the agenda and encouraging socializing online this year.\n   </figcaption></img>\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>If you’re not planning to have any audience interaction in your webinar, then why not just play a recording? The whole reason you do it live is because you want people to interact and engage with each other.</p> \n<p>This means doing more than just a 15-minute Q&amp;A at the end of each presentation, though. Try incorporating live polls into your webinar to engage with attendees as they’re watching. Get people in the chat room talking by having pre-prepared conversation topics that relate back to the topics you’re covering. Think outside the typical mold of a webinar to get your audience engaged.</p> \n<p><strong>Make It Seamless</strong></p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/GoToWebinar-Settings.jpg\" alt=\"The backend of a webinar platform.\" class=\"wp-image-96526\" width=\"960\" height=\"488\">\n   <figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">\n    Use your webinar platform to create a seamless experience for attendees.\n   </figcaption></img>\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>“Pay no attention to the man behind the curtain!” In a great webinar or online event, you don’t see all the work that’s going on behind the scenes. Try to make things as seamless as possible for attendees by paying close attention to what their experience looks and feels like.</p> \n<p>Have a welcome message ready for each session, prep your host with some topics of conversation to fill time in between segments, and monitor for audience engagement in the chat and on social media. Depending on the size of your event, you’ll want at least two or three people working in the background to keep things running smoothly.</p> \n<p><strong>Make It Surprising</strong></p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/call-to-action-conference-2016-high-five-1.jpg\" alt=\"High-fives at CTAConf.\" class=\"wp-image-96526\" width=\"960\" height=\"488\">\n   <figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">\n    We go all out for in-person conferences. Why not treat your online events the same way?\n   </figcaption></img>\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>Think about some of the most memorable moments you’ve had at conferences in the past. It’s usually the stuff that you’re not expecting that sticks out, even years later. A delightful curveball—like when there’s a lineup of over-caffeinated Unbouncers ready to high-five you as you walk into <a href=\"https://calltoactionconference.unbounce.com/\">CTAConf</a>.</p> \n<p>Brainstorm some ways you can surprise attendees and speakers with swag, giveaways, games, or activities. It can be a great way to break up a busy day, and help you go beyond that regular old webinar experience.</p> \n<h2 id=\"Tip8\">8. Follow Through Post-Event</h2> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/thinkific-think-in-colour-facebook.jpg\" alt=\"A Facebook Group attached to an online event.\" class=\"wp-image-96526\" width=\"960\" height=\"488\">\n   <figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">\n    Thinkific created an \n    <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://unbounce.com/campaign-strategy/thinkific-using-landing-pages-double-saas-growth/\">online community</a> after their virtual summit to continue the conversation (and keep leads engaged).\n   </figcaption></img>\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>Now that your webinar is over, you can put your feet up on the desk and relax, right? No way—there’s still one more important step that would make you smack your forehead if you forgot.</p> \n<p>Because you don’t want the experience to just be over and forgotten by everyone, follow up with attendees (and registrants who couldn’t make it) afterward to provide any relevant materials or webinar recordings. This will give you another opportunity to track who is engaged and interested in this content—and who might fit into an email nurture to eventually become a customer.</p> \n<p>You might also want to consider creating a Facebook Group or a Slack Community Channel to keep the conversation alive between your speakers and attendees. That’s what Thinkific did after their <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.thinkific.com/thinkincolor2020/\" target=\"_blank\">Think in Color Online Summit</a>—and they now have an additional channel that can reach <strong>over 1,700 members</strong>. (Check out the <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/campaign-strategy/thinkific-using-landing-pages-double-saas-growth/\">full customer story</a> for more details on how they got those numbers.)</p> \n<p>Oh, and don’t forget to follow up and thank your speakers too! Sidekick","link":"https://unbounce.com/?p=98264","description":"\n<p>“You’ve got to do <strong>more</strong> with <strong>less</strong>.” If you’re running a small business or marketing agency, this isn’t some theoretical paradox or <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ReFhu8KYbmU\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Goblin King riddle</a>—this is actual advice you’ll hear on how to grow your revenue. The fastest way to scale up is to take on more clients and customers. But somehow you have to do that <em>without</em> taking on more expenses or sacrificing on the work you’re already delivering.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Sounds impossible, right?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Maybe not. <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/conversion-intelligence/\">Conversion Intelligence</a> is helping to level the playing field for small business owners and savvy marketers alike. You might not have the same resources as those bigger, enterprise companies you’re competing with—but you do have access to AI and machine learning tools that can help you deliver <strong>higher-converting campaigns</strong> with <strong>fewer resources</strong>.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>This is something that Mats Moy, digital marketing consultant and founder of <a href=\"https://matsmoy.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Moy Consulting</a>, knows from experience. For years, Mats has been helping roofing companies generate online leads and become authorities in their local markets. But as a one-man show, he has had to spend a lot of his time juggling multiple different clients and projects, while also being responsible for the marketing of his own business.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/large-Blog_SmartTraffic_Portrait_1.png\" alt=\"Mats Moy, Moy Consulting\" class=\"wp-image-98289\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/large-Blog_SmartTraffic_Portrait_1.png 1364w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/large-Blog_SmartTraffic_Portrait_1-150x110.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/large-Blog_SmartTraffic_Portrait_1-341x250.png 341w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/large-Blog_SmartTraffic_Portrait_1-80x59.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/large-Blog_SmartTraffic_Portrait_1-768x563.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/large-Blog_SmartTraffic_Portrait_1-1000x733.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/large-Blog_SmartTraffic_Portrait_1-650x477.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/large-Blog_SmartTraffic_Portrait_1-300x220.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/large-Blog_SmartTraffic_Portrait_1-160x117.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1364px) 100vw, 1364px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Around November 2019 though, everything changed for Mats. (Dun, dun, dunnn.) Since then, he has seen his business grow <strong>five times larger</strong> with the help of Unbounce landing pages and our AI-powered optimization tool, <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/product/smart-traffic/\">Smart Traffic</a>. And this level of success is something Mats says he’s still coming to terms with&#8230;</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"blog-photo\"><img class=\"alignright size-full wp-image-96860\" src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_SmartTraffic_Quote_Portrait.jpg\" alt=\"Mats Moy, Moy Consulting\" width=\"83\" height=\"83\"/></a></div>\n\n\n\n<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote\"><p>I haven&#8217;t heard too many people speak about this feeling. Keep reading to hear more about the lead gen method he used to grow his consultancy, and how he’s been able to keep his operation lean and high-converting with tools like Unbounce.</p>\n\n\n\n<h2><strong>Lots of Opportunities, But Limited Resources</strong></h2>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/No-Payne-Roofing-LP.png\" alt=\"A roofing landing page example\" class=\"wp-image-96526\" width=\"960\" height=\"488\"><figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">A single conversion on a roofing landing page can drive anywhere between $6,000 and $10,000 in revenue. That’s a lot of shingles—er, I mean singles!</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>When Mats first started his marketing consulting business, he immediately saw the benefit of getting his clients to use landing pages. A typical roof replacement will normally run somewhere between $6,000 and $10,000, which makes every <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/solutions/use-case/ppc/\">PPC ad click</a> incredibly valuable.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"blog-photo\"><img class=\"alignright size-full wp-image-96860\" src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_SmartTraffic_Quote_Portrait.jpg\" alt=\"Mats Moy, Moy Consulting\" width=\"83\" height=\"83\"/></a></div>\n\n\n\n<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote\"><p>Traffic-wise, this is not an industry where you&#8217;ll see thousands of hits a day. Roofing clicks are very expensive, right? Your typical paid ads campaign from Google might be like 10 cents, 30 cents, or maybe a dollar for a click. But in roofing, some [in this industry] are paying like 60 bucks or more per click. So it&#8217;s quite pricey.</p></blockquote>\n\n\n\n<p>By creating <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/product/landing-pages/\">landing pages</a> that targeted specific local keywords (e.g., “affordable roofing in Calgary”), Mats was able to help his clients earn more revenue from their ad spends and dominate their local markets. It was a super-effective strategy—he could test and optimize much faster on landing pages and get higher conversion rates compared to competitors who were still sending traffic to their websites.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>But there was a (metaphorical) ceiling that blocked how much Mats could grow this business. He simply couldn’t be everywhere at once, and hiring loads more people wasn’t an option for him at this stage.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"blog-photo\"><img class=\"alignright size-full wp-image-96860\" src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_SmartTraffic_Quote_Portrait.jpg\" alt=\"Mats Moy, Moy Consulting\" width=\"83\" height=\"83\"/></a></div>\n\n\n\n<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote\"><p>What were my resources like? Well, I was by myself. A one-man show doing absolutely everything. And I think I was juggling maybe like four or five clients at a time doing all the work using landing pages. You gotta move really quickly when you&#8217;re first starting out.</p></blockquote>\n\n\n\n<p>Mats knew that something had to change if he was ever going to expand his business and grow his revenue. So, he started brainstorming some of the different ways he could generate leads to attract more roofing clients—without giving him a ton of extra work on the side.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"blog-photo\"><img class=\"alignright size-full wp-image-96860\" src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_SmartTraffic_Quote_Portrait.jpg\" alt=\"Mats Moy, Moy Consulting\" width=\"83\" height=\"83\"/></a></div>\n\n\n\n<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote\"><p>Late last year, I set a goal for myself. ‘We&#8217;re going to reach X amount of customers.’ And step by step, I set out to make it happen. And it was just bull at that stage, it was just an idea. But then you start working on it and over time you slowly start to see &#8230; Whoa, this is working.</p></blockquote>\n\n\n\n<h2><strong>A Lead Generation Training Course Powered by Smart Traffic<img src=\"https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/12.0.0-1/72x72/2122.png\" alt=\"™\" class=\"wp-smiley\" style=\"height: 1em; max-height: 1em;\" /></strong></h2>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Moy-Consulting-Homepage.png\" alt=\"The Moy Consulting training program for roofers\" class=\"wp-image-98322\" srcset=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Moy-Consulting-Homepage.png 2528w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Moy-Consulting-Homepage-150x63.png 150w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Moy-Consulting-Homepage-560x235.png 560w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Moy-Consulting-Homepage-80x34.png 80w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Moy-Consulting-Homepage-768x322.png 768w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Moy-Consulting-Homepage-1536x644.png 1536w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Moy-Consulting-Homepage-2048x859.png 2048w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Moy-Consulting-Homepage-1000x419.png 1000w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Moy-Consulting-Homepage-650x273.png 650w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Moy-Consulting-Homepage-300x126.png 300w, https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Moy-Consulting-Homepage-160x67.png 160w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2528px) 100vw, 2528px\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>To attract even more clients, Mats decided to turn his agency model on its head and start teaching roofers how to market for themselves. He figured that if they could use a mouse, they could build a landing page in Unbounce.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"blog-photo\"><img class=\"alignright size-full wp-image-96860\" src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_SmartTraffic_Quote_Portrait.jpg\" alt=\"Mats Moy, Moy Consulting\" width=\"83\" height=\"83\"/></a></div>\n\n\n\n<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote\"><p>I needed a tool that would be easy not just for myself, but also for my clients to use. Because when it comes to roofers with computers&#8230; it just scares them. Like someone could barely copy and paste or turn on a computer, but here we are creating Unbounce landing pages!</p></blockquote>\n\n\n\n<p>And because Mats was a part of the <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/partner-program/\">Unbounce Partner Program</a>, he was able to offer any roofers who took his training program a 20% discount off their first three months using Unbounce. In exchange, he would earn <strong>20% recurring revenue for every referral</strong>.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"blog-photo\"><img class=\"alignright size-full wp-image-96860\" src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_SmartTraffic_Quote_Portrait.jpg\" alt=\"Mats Moy, Moy Consulting\" width=\"83\" height=\"83\"/></a></div>\n\n\n\n<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote\"><p>I launched [the training program] back in November, and that&#8217;s been my sole focus. Rather than get bogged down in the day-to-day management of each new client, he would be able to set them up with the skills, strategies, and tools to be successful online (and then offer his services to help them keep scaling). Like the old adage says, “Give a roofer a fish, and you feed them for a day. But give a roofer a crash course in landing pages, and you feed them for life.”</p>\n\n\n\n<p>To get the word out about his new training program, Mats decided to use a series of Facebook Ads that would specifically target roofers. He used long-form storytelling to get their attention, and then routed them to a registration landing page to sign up for more details.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Facebook-Ad-Moy-Consulting.png\" alt=\"An example of a Facebook ad Mats used to attract leads\" class=\"wp-image-96526\" width=\"960\" height=\"488\"><figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">Mats uses long-form storytelling in his Facebook ads to get the attention of roofers.</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>But Mats wasn’t sending roofers to any old landing page—he was sending them to a landing page powered by <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/product/smart-traffic/\">Unbounce Smart Traffic</a><img src=\"https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/12.0.0-1/72x72/2122.png\" alt=\"™\" class=\"wp-smiley\" style=\"height: 1em; max-height: 1em;\" />. This was key because Mats was still juggling a lot of responsibilities in his role. He had to run the training course <em>and</em> manage his clients, so he didn’t want to be running small-scale A/B tests on his lunch break, too.</p>\n\n\n<div class=\"editors-note\">\n    <p><strong>What’s the Smart Traffic advantage?</strong> Using machine learning, Smart Traffic boosts your conversion rates by <em>automagically</em> sending visitors to the landing page variant that&#8217;s most relevant. These split-second routing decisions are more accurate than a human-powered test and eliminate most of the manual hassles—and long wait times—marketers associate with traditional testing. <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/product/smart-traffic/\">Learn more about how Smart Traffic works here</a>.</p>\n</div>\n\n\n<p>Instead, Mats whipped up a bunch of different variants to test new headlines and imagery on the page. Then, he used the Unbounce machine learning algorithm to automatically route visitors to the version they were most likely to convert on. No muss, no fuss.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Moy-Consulting-Smart-Traffic-Variants.png\" alt=\"Smart Traffic variants testing different headlines for Moy Consulting\" class=\"wp-image-96526\" width=\"960\" height=\"488\"><figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">Some of the different headlines Mats is testing with Smart Traffic. If you’re really busy, or you don&#8217;t have that optimization experience, Smart Traffic will be your new best friend. It&#8217;s using machine learning to help you get those better results.</p></blockquote>\n\n\n\n<h2><strong>Blowing the Roof Off With 5x Growth in 6 Months</strong></h2>\n\n\n\n<p>Six months later, Mats has gone from having <strong>15 clients to over 80</strong>. And while this type of breakneck growth might have been unsustainable for him before, the lead gen training course has proven to be a reliable source of new leads for his business. He’s netting an 8% conversion rate on the registration landing page and seeing <strong>a conversion lift of over 35% with the help of Smart Traffic</strong>. (In other words, he&#8217;d be getting less than a 6% conversion rate if he were running these variants in a traditional A/B test.)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>This has given Mats the confidence to <strong>grow his team and bring on four other marketers</strong> to assist with Moy Consulting. (Which means he can also finally put away his juggling gloves, because this is no longer a one-man show.)</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"blog-photo\"><img class=\"alignright size-full wp-image-96860\" src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_SmartTraffic_Quote_Portrait.jpg\" alt=\"Mats Moy, Moy Consulting\" width=\"83\" height=\"83\"/></a></div>\n\n\n\n<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote\"><p>Clients are happy with the program. I have people raving about it. So they&#8217;re seeing leads. It&#8217;s unlike anything that&#8217;s out there. And that&#8217;s the best part, knowing that your success comes from the success of your clients. That’s awesome.</p></blockquote>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full is-resized\"><img src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Moy-Consulting-Smart-Traffic-Metrics.png\" alt=\"The Unbounce dashboard showing a Smart Traffic conversion lift\" class=\"wp-image-96526\" width=\"960\" height=\"488\"><figcaption class=\"blog-photo-annotation\">Mats is seeing a conversion lift of over 35% (!!!) with Smart Traffic.</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Speaking of client success, Mats is also using Smart Traffic on his clients’ roofing pages too. In some cases, he’s been able to bring the cost-per-lead down from <strong>$160 to as low as $40</strong>, and <strong>get conversion rates as high as 19% (with an incredible 70% lift from Smart Traffic)</strong>. That’s well above the 2.6% median for the home improvement industry, according to the <a href=\"https://unbounce.com/conversion-benchmark-report/#about_this_report\">2020 Conversion Benchmark Report</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"blog-photo\"><img class=\"alignright size-full wp-image-96860\" src=\"https://mk0zofoqaluvgdskgvsb.kinstacdn.com/photos/Blog_SmartTraffic_Quote_Portrait.jpg\" alt=\"Mats Moy, Moy Consulting\" width=\"83\" height=\"83\"/></a></div>\n\n\n\n<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote\"><p>You can hear it in my voice&#8230; I&#8217;m pretty damn proud of some of the metrics that we&#8217;ve been able to gather and get from these campaigns.</p></blockquote>\n\n\n\n<p>For marketers still on the fence about Smart Traffic, Mats says he gets it.
